puis escorche le cuir qui est entre les II levres, et oste la graisse, et i amenistre ceu que nos avons dit de costure et de poudres, et ceu qui est necessaire en la cure, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then scorches the skin between the two lips, and removes the fat, and applies what we have said about stitching and powders, and whatever is necessary for the treatment, until he is healed;
et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	and if he is not healed, or the incision is not fully made, because the patient will not rest, or due to bleeding, you should fill the wound with wet cotton soaked in corrosive ointment;
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	and let it remain until it dissolves the remainder and the fat, then treat it until he is healed.
des apostemes des asselles	of abscesses of the armpits
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	These abscesses that come from under the armpits are like hard scrofula and they have nodules, and some contain moisture.
Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	Those who retain moisture must be cut according to this form, from line b to line g:
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when all the content of the abscess is drained, then fill the wound with clean cotton, and leave it until the next day; then remove all the cotton and dress it with suitable ointment until it heals.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the abscesses are like scrofula, then treat them as we have said for fissures of scrofula, and if the wound is closed, then administer cautery as we have said before.
de la routure de l’artere	of the rupture of the artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	When an artery is severed, and the skin on top is sutured, it often results in abscesses, and likewise, the vein becomes swollen and abscessed;
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	and if one knows it is due to an artery, then the abscesses are long and deep;
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	and when you feel it with your fingers, you will feel the dislocation;
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	and when it is in the vein, there is a visible swelling;
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	and it is foolish to cover this abscess, especially when it is under the armpits and in the groin, neck, and many other places, and is very large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	Therefore, one should avoid cauterizing with iron, and the one who is on top should also be avoided, and in the one who has inflammation of an artery that opens above the skin of the neck;
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	then operate with a knife, and cut the artery from the threads well, so that it is exposed;et puis fent un trou au chief de la pize, si grand com ele soit;
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	then make a hole in the head of the stone, as large as it is; then put an awl under it, and pierce it through to the other side, and tie the artery with a double thread in two places, according to how I instructed you in the extraction of the two arteries that are in the temples;et si c’est une pize que ne se puet aler, et ele est trop grosse, covient le fendre, et aler l’artere qui soit dedenz, et la tyier;
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	then point the location between the two strings of an introducer so that the pus flows out and the abscess is drained.
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	then apply the treatment that dries up pus, until the wound drains;
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat with ointment appropriate for this, until it is healed;
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	and if the abscess is due to the size of the wound, you should dye your hand with something from the abscess all over the skin, then insert a needle under the area you're holding, and thread a double length of string through it, so that you can pull it from the other side;
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	then tie off the abscess, as I've told you, tying one end of the string to each shoulder;
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	and if you're worried the string might slip out, insert another needle through the entire length of the string under the abscess at the incision of the first needle, and tie the strings in four places;
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	then scrape the abscess until the excess fluid drains out, then scrape off the excess from the wound and leave what is stuck to it.
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then place a damp cloth soaked in wine and oil over the wound, then apply poultices and ointments until it is healed.
des apostemes des ners	of abscesses of the nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Also, as abscesses come in the artery and vein, they also come in the nerves when they are injured, or from too great exertion, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	This happens most often at the shoulders and in all joints where there is an abscess, and its color resembles that of the body, and it has various appearances without pain;
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	and when you press it firmly, it hurts, and it is not deep in the body but under the skin;
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	and it cannot move in any direction, neither forward nor backward, nor downward nor upward, and that which is in joints should not be cauterized with iron:
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	for there may be contraction;
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	and that which is on the head or forehead, use the spiderwort plant.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, hold it with tweezers and squeeze it at its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if it is large, they suspend it with a hook, and cut it open, then remove the bone and sew up the wound until it heals.
des grosses boces pendans	of large, hanging
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	Sometimes it occurs in bellies and nowhere else, and is a disease called "mushroom" due to its resemblance to mushrooms, with thin roots and thick stems;
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	and there are both small and very large ones;
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	and I saw one man who had two in his belly that looked more like mushrooms than anything else, and there was no difference between them, and they were white, and had thin roots, and were slightly cracked, and moisture ran out of them.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I cut them open and found one weighing 18 ounces and the other 6 ounces, and the procedure for incising is to look at the wound if it is moist, and the color of the joint is white and moist with thin roots;
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	if the blade of the spatule is wide, and have the fire cautery ready in your presence.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For in cutting there are often excessive bleedings of blood, and if it bleeds profusely, then hasten to the cautery.
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	and if you see the patient frightened and fearful of the incision with the knife, take a well-prepared thread, tie it around the tendon as we have said, and leave it for two days;
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	and then release it, and keep tightening the thread until the tendon is cut without pain;
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	and if the roots are large, there is fear of cutting near the belly as well, but you can cut half of it, then cauterize it so that it does not grow back.
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	Then treat the wound and be careful not to cut the skin which is of a bluish color and poor in feeling and of milky appearance.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is a deep abscess, and I will come to the treatment of ulcers next.
quant li boude ist fuer	when the boil has burst
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the appearance of a hernia comes from cauterization of a wound or from a fissure in the syphilis, and it is on the abdomen and some of the bowels, as it happens in other routings, or from blood flowing from veins or arteries according to what is before, or from flatulence;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	and if it is from the syphilis routing and from the bowel output, then the color of the abscess is similar to the color of the body, and it is a minor thing without pain, and it opens with various outputs.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is from the exit of the intestine, then it is more diverse, and when one presses it with their fingers, it pops out, and then returns in, and sometimes it is dried up, and increases a lot at the entrance of the bath and through hard work.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	And if it is due to moisture, it is a minor thing, and it opens well when you press it with your hand, and it does not constrict at all;Et se li bouez sont desaloiez de lor lieu, et li chiés adoun desaloiez, si convient que tu les remettes a lor
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	And if the bowels are dislocated from their place, and the head is also dislocated, then you must reset them to their place;and if it is due to blood, then the large and hard abscesses open according to a certain quantity;Et se c’est par ventositeit, si convient que tu
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	and if it is due to windiness, then it is soft in the touch, and the works are such that you look to see whether the appearance is from the blood of the artery, or the vein, or windiness.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	If you are to leave the wound untreated, then:
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear, as I told you in the chapter on abscesses, regarding both the artery and the vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	And if the appearance is from the intestines or the belly, then it is necessary that you command the patient to tighten his armpit, and be stretched out straight, then sign all around the pit;
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	then command him to lie down soon between your hands, then go around the place that you have signed all over the spatumile, then put half of the abscess at the top to all the great hook;
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	then tie it around with a strong thread, or a strong silk rope firmly, and let the navel be absolved;
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	then work half of the stretched abscess on the string, and put in your index finger, and seek the intestine;
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	If you find it caught in the bowel, loosen it and push the intestine back into the abdomen.
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	And if you find the bowels blocked, grab them at the anus, and cut off the excess.
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	And if the arteries are contrary to you, or the vein, go around gently, then return to your work and take two needles, and thread two strong threads, and thread the two needles through what you have done in a cross shape that you are piercing.
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	Then stretch the abscess in four places on the needles, and if you see, remove the needles, and leave it so that it may drain, and push out the dead flesh by itself.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	Or cut it when it is subtle and drainage, then clean it as necessary, and bandage the abscess as we have said.
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	And extract the blood or moisture which you find, then clean the area as it should be, and close the wound.
dou chancre	for sores
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have discussed in the previous section the appearance of sores, and how one should treat them with medication, and how one must avoid using an iron cautery;
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	and we will now discuss sores that appear on the testicles, and the great caution one must take in treating them, according to the ancients. When sores appear on places where they can be scratched, like on the breasts, thighs, and similar areas, and when they are in their initial stage, they should all be removed.
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	But when they become large and old, one must not approach them, for I have never seen anyone healed from them.And if sores appear on the head or face, one should use a medicine to remove them, and if they are deep, one should fill them with white lead and wax, and cover them until they heal.If there is a
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	I have never seen anyone heal from this.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And the operation, when it is in a place where it can be removed, as we have said, is that you sometimes cleanse the patient of black bile.
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	Then have him bleed if he shows signs of fullness, then ease the pain in the affected area to perform the operation.
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	Then inspect his genitals and anus, and the head from all sides, leaving nothing untouched;
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	and let the blood flow out freely, and squeeze the area with your hand or something else, and if the blood flow is contrary to the incision of the artery or vein, cauterize it until the bleeding stops.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat him again until he is healed.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have already described the types of dropsy, how the accumulation of fluid occurs, and the signs of each type, as well as the treatment through medicine and surgery.
si est eclites soulement;	if it is only scalded;
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	and one must not touch with iron in these two cases:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	that is to say, tympany and ipohondria, for they are deadly things;
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	therefore when you treat this appearance of dropsy which is called 'scalded' with medicines, and the treatment does not help, look to see if the patient is weak, or if he has another illness than dropsy, such as thirst and stomachache, and similar things;
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	do not touch with iron, for there is doubt in it;
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	and if you see the patient is very strong, and he has no other illness but dropsy alone, and he is not too young or too old, then you must work thus:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	let the patient lie on his back in your arms, and press his stomach upwards by pushing the water to the lowest part of his feet; then take the spatiumile with thorns according to this form:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let there be two parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	with a point, and yet not so sharp that it can reach the intestines when thrust in, nor cause bleeding.
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	then examine whether the dropsy is localized towards the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	if you should cut into the buttock three fingers deep directly under the hip bone;
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	and if the dropsy is due to liver disease, then your cut should be at the left side of the buttock three fingers deep;
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	and if it's due to kidney disease, then it should be on the right side, and the patient must not lie on the cut so that the excess fluids do not flow into that weak area;
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	then pierce through the skin with your instrument, and insert it, and lift your hand to all the spatumile between the skin and the syfac as much as an inch or so deep;
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	then pierce the syphilis until the sputum comes to the surface, and that is the source of the pus, then pull it out, and insert this instrument from which comes the shape:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it is similar to a thin silver rod, and is made of light bronze or brass, and has at the bottom a small hole:
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and on one side, it has three holes;
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and two on the other, and one on the other;
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	and the end is shaped like a feather, and that is the shape of the incision from which the scribes cut feathers:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	at the top there is a groove, so that when the instrument comes to the pus, it will immediately go onto the instrument;
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	so draw off half or a third, for if you draw off more than is proper in that hour, by chance the patient may die from the shock to his spirit, or he will faint, or he will approach death;
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but empty according to the quantity of its virtue, and according to what the dispositions of the virtue of the malady signify, and his pulses;
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	then treat the instrument and retain the water, which is now retained by the plug that blocks the hole on the syphilis, about which I have spoken, that you pierce according to this manner;
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	then restart the instrument the next day, if you see the patient suffering from that, and treat a little water;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	do this every day, and keep applying until there is no more water but a little bit of water.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you doubt the patient, and leave a lot of water, then treat with hot sand or sachet, and by much sweating or bathing and in the sun, and drink tea;

de l’estopement de la verge	of the stopping of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born without a foreskin, or with a small foreskin, or one that is not in its proper place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	If necessary, cut into the foreskin with a very thin knife according to this method:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	then place a small, fine plug of wool in the urethra, and tie it and hold it there for three or four days. When he wants to urinate, remove the plug and let him urinate, then replace the plug.
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	Perhaps this is not necessary, because the pus that comes out will not allow it to close.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	Those whose foreskin is small, if they are circumcised with a sharp knife, as we have said, will enlarge.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those who do not have an opening in their place are bloated, because some are born with the opening at the head of the penis, which prevents them from urinating until they lift their penis upwards.

Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the manner of the operation is that the patient lies on his back, then the top of the rod and the cup are also as big as a feather, so that the hole piece in the middle, as it should be.
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	And beware of bleeding that often occurs, and if it happens, then stop the flow of blood from whoever is bleeding, and cure the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	of pustules on the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	Many times these warts come on the penis, and they are an ugly-looking growth;
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	and there are both malicious and harmless ones;
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	so you should grab them with a needle subtly, and cut and clean all of them, then put cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment on top;
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	then cure it with diaphenicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the ulcer is malignant, discolored and putrid, then you must apply cautery.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have cut it, and if the wart is on the head of the penis, and part of it is inside the skin and part outside, then you should remove the wart that is inside first;
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	And when it is sewed up, then heal it.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	For when you sew it up together, the scrotum is not secure so it can be pierced, and blackness and corruption come in his penis and testicles;
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	You must cut out all that is black and rotten, then apply a plaster of honey and wheat flour made from pomegranate bark and fennel, then heal it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if there is bleeding, use the lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	Cauteries have two uses together: l’un est qu’il tue la carne corrumpute et li maux
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	One is that it kills rotten flesh and the disease, that is, in bloodletting and corruption; l’auter si est a la dislocation, que il rassoie li
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	The other is for dislocation, to smooth the joints and if the scrotum is rotten and retracted, you must insert a rod into the penis, and the patient will urinate through it.
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	and when the foreskin is swollen at the head of the penis, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, or due to a wound or abscess, you must therefore scrape it with a sharp instrument, as far as the ligature, and free the glans of the penis all around;
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	and if it is a serious matter to discuss this, you must scrape it with a sharp spatula or knife, starting from the head of the penis and moving down;
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	then gently pull it apart and place a thin damp linen cloth in the opening to prevent it from swelling again.
de la circoncision	of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision is not a dislocation like other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Nevertheless, when we perform this operation by choice, and properly on children, it is necessary to do the best and most gentle work for their safety.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not mention the circumcision of their infants, for they did not practice it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired through experimentation.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For I have seen most of the masters and healers who perform circumcision around the glans, and on foreskins, and on all new-borns.
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	if it were the hernia because there are two membranes, and by chance one is above and the other below.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Then they cover it, and the pain is doubled, and in the purification which is done on the glans is not assured, the end of the member.
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	and in the purification of the nail, by accident the iron slips and they ruin the work, and many times they are born so that they don't need purification, and I have seen it.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the purification that is done forcefully all around the thread of hair, I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the forces cut justly both above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand, you cut evenly all around.
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	but the thread should be well wound around the skin.
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	and the manner of the first work is that you should make the child think, if he hears, that you only tie the thread around the penis, and then you let him go in all the ways you can;
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	then make it stand upright between your hands, and conceal the strength between your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see them, nor any of the tools.
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	then put your hand on the penis and breathe or cough, and pull it upwards until the head of the penis is exposed;
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	then cleanse it well of the dirt that has accumulated there, then tie the cut area with a double thread, then tie it under the scrotum to the other testicle;
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	and hold it by the testicles with your index finger and thumb, and press between the two threads, then quickly lift the foreskin and pull the head of the penis;
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	then let the blood flow little by little, because it is the venom;
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and place powder on top and on top of the powder a cloth glued with a roasted egg yolk tempered with rose water, cooked in good and fresh rosemary oil, and let it stay until the next day, and then treat it again until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The form of forces for purification is as follows:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	the two knives should be thin and sharp, and the handles should be as long as the palm equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	The mistake in purification is when the blood vessels inside are cut during the incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	Therefore, you must stretch it with your fingernail, so that the skin becomes an abscess;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	and grasp it evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, then hold it with tweezers, and then grasp it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if it lasts for 3 days, and what is under the skin is swollen, then leave it until the abscess is relieved and the skin is lightly scraped;
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	then grasp it as you can, and beware of the part of the penis, it will not harm him in any way.Et s’il est desoz la verge enflez, si le laisse tant que li aposteme soit apaisiez; et li vout quier en l’end
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Therefore treat the site of sudden wounds with powder, as we have said in the treatise on powders, and if one applies it too generously, and it goes above, it will do no harm.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And cure it, therefore, as we have said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	from the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to a stone, or frozen blood, or bowels, or unformed matter, or similar things that we have described in the division.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	And if the urine is not loosened and you see that it is retained by a stone which is stuck in the neck of the bladder, then you must have the patient bend his knees;
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	and place his feet on his back, and arch his belly from the part above his back, and restrain the patient's breathing as hard as he can;
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	and then the neck of the bladder is compressed to express the stone above, causing the urine to be released;
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come out as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must use an instrument called a 'syringe' to extract it. The syringe is made thus:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	It should be made of thin silver wire, like the feather of a bird;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	The tube should be about a palm and a half in length, and thin at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And to make the urine flow out in this way, you must take a length of double thread and tie a small plug of wool or cotton onto it. Then insert the tip of the thread into the syringe;
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	and cover the excess wool with oil or butter and a little egg white, then have the patient sit on a chair. Then anoint his bladder and penis with moist oil or olive oil and warm water;
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	then place the syringe gently into the penis, until it reaches the root of the penis, then double the penis upwards towards the scrotum;
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	then fill the syringe before it reaches the bladder, and the patient will feel the pain travel to the empty space; if this is not done according to this order, then because the person guiding where it goes is wrong;
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	then tightly wind the thread all around the wool, and urine will follow the wool, then pull it out, and make the urine flow;
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and use the syringe again until the bladder is emptied and the pain is alleviated.
des maladies de la vessie	of diseases of the bladder:
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When burns or blood come in the bladder, or pus is accumulated there, and you see water and medicine distilling, then do this to all of the instrument that is called "clepsydra", and it is formed:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed and has three openings:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	two on one side and one on the other, as you can see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	and the hair-like channels through which the medicine passes must be such that it blocks the penis without addition, and one can milk out moisture and fill when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	and when you see your medicine flowing in the bladder, place the tip of the syringe into the moisture, and draw out what is inside.
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	then suck up the moisture with the syringe, and then close off the opening firmly.
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	if it enters inside, it will now reach the bladder, and the patient will feel it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	and this is how you prepare the subtle enema to cleanse the bladder:
si est ci:	take:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	A vessel made of silver or brass, with its spout pointing upwards;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and below it has a hole or slit;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	then take a lamb's bladder and place it on the fire to heat up, along with the water you intend to use for the enema. Tie the bladder with a strong thread, making sure the knot is tight;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	then insert the tip of the enema into the penis, and squeeze your hand over the bladder to release the water gradually, until the patient feels it has reached his bladder.
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	and if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment, make it into a circle, and pierce it evenly all around.
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	then thread a strong wire through these holes, then assemble the circle as one would assemble a ball, and put inside what you wish of oil and moisture and water, and fasten it in the instrument.
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and do as you did with the bladder, squeezing by hand until the moisture comes to the bladder.
de la piere	of the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have already discussed in the division of stones the methods and extraction together with medicines;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	and I said the difference between a stone in the kidney, and all the signs, and which kind of stone one must operate on;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	and I will tell you openly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the stone which is lodged in the bladder occurs more often in children, and it is a sign that the water jumps from the bladder like water in its subtlety;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	And he pulls out the hair, and twists his scrotum, and he hurts him many times, and then he stops.
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and this causes the foundations to crumble;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and healing is quick in children until they are four years old, and it is slow in the elderly, and it is moderate in those between youth and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	and the cure is quicker in those who have large stones than in those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is fitting first to cleanse the patient through enema, to draw out all the feces which are in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes blocks the search for the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet and lift him up and move him around so that the stone sinks to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it will come out from above;
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	then let him sit between your hands, with his hands under his thighs so that the bladder is completely tilted downwards;
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	then feel and touch inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	if you feel the stone within the cavity, then you must cut upon the stone now.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not give way to pressure, then wet your left index finger with oil, if the patient is adult, or your middle finger if the patient is young;
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and insert it into his anus, and feel for the stone within his urethra, and when you feel it with your finger, draw it gently into the bladder's neck;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	then press upon your finger, and the stone will move out of the way where you intend to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the assistant to press upon the bladder with his hand, and tell him to extend the scrotum upwards with his right hand, and with his left hand pull back the skin underneath the testicles in the area where the incision will be made;
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	then insert the spatulum, which is curved in shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And they do so between what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but to the side of the left arse cheek.
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	and be straight on the stone, and your fingers be close to the anus, and the incision should be diagonal so that it is wide at the top and narrow at the bottom, according to the size of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	by chance the pressure from the fingers which are by the anus may cause it to jump out without effort.
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and know that there is such a stone where there are edges and margins:
si est griés a issir;	if it is easy to push out;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	and some which are underneath, similar to a grape, and round, whose passage is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	For those therefore where there are edges and margins, make the incision larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if it does not jump out, then you must hold steady with tweezers which are as sharp as a knife at the tip, to extract the stone so that it does not escape;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	or you put underneath the instrument a subtle bandage on the head;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot trick it in this way, then widen the hole, and if there is bleeding, then stop it with vitriol;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there is more than one stone, then stop the largest at the neck of the bladder first, then cut above it, then pull it out, and then the smaller ones after it if there are several.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then it must be seared, and a larger wound made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For there are two things that happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	either he dies or the urine comes out through the wound where the urethra cannot heal;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but nevertheless, try to pull it out, or tear it with pincers, pulling it out in pieces;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	and when you have finished your work, stop the bleeding with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, and hold it steady, then put on a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine, or in oil and rosewater and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess;
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	then treat the patient on his neck, and do not loosen the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen it, wash the area well with oil and water, then treat the wound with thin ointment and thick ointment until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if abscesses, scabs and blood clots come to the wound and congelation of blood in the bladder, and there is retention of urine due to this, known in such a way that without salt with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	then put your finger into the wound and extract that blood, for if it remains there, it will corrupt the bladder and destroy it.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then cleanse the wound with water, vinegar and salt, and assist the patient in every way you know until he is healed.
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	and it is necessary that every hour as you treat him, to tie his two thighs together and apply the medication on the affected area.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small and located in the passage of the penis, pierced through it and let the urine flow out.
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	if the patient with such an injury, which you treat many times, is then excused from further treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have tried this before.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take an iron needle with three pointed ends and insert it into a hot brand:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	Then take a thread and tie it around the base of the stone so that it cannot return to the bladder.
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	Then push the wire into the base gently until it reaches the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and turn the wire in your hand within the stone little by little until you can pierce the stone from the other side;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	then urine will flow immediately, then press your hand on what is remaining of the stone within the wire.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	If it is broken at once and comes out with the urine, the patient is healed;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	and if you cannot do this due to any resistance, tie a wire underneath the stone and another one above it, then push the wire between the stones with both wires in place, then pull it out, untie the wires and clean the congealed blood in the wound;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of women's stones
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	It sometimes happens that a stone becomes impacted in women, and if it does, the treatment is difficult, and it is prohibited for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	one is that the woman may be a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second is that one cannot find a skilled woman who will undergo examination, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third reason is that one may not be able to find a skilled woman in this art of medicine;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	and the fourth reason is that the woman's stone is often deeper than a man's, so a deeper incision is required, and there is greater fear involved. And if necessity demands it, you should press a skilled midwife into service, and with great difficulty force her to do so, and if you cannot find such a midwife, then a wise and cunning but unchaste woman will suffice;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and have a wise woman examine her, or a woman who knows something of medicine, and instruct her to do what you tell her from your examination of the stone.
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and be sure to check if the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then she should push out her bowel and search for the stone.
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, then she should push on her abdomen and constrict under her navel, and recommend that she push out her bowel or as the patient needs, and press her left hand firmly on her bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, then she should move it inch by inch from the entrance of the bladder all the way down to the root of the thigh.
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Then she should press on the stone at the root of the thigh against the middle of the urethra, where it is most sensitive, and feel for the stone in that area.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and do not move your hand above or below the stone, and make the incision small at first;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then open the incision wider if you feel that the stone is cutting into the wound so much that it can come out, and know that there are many kinds of stones;
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	that is to say, small and large, rough and smooth, long and round, and they come in many shapes.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	you will know what to look for in order to identify the type of stone.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the blood flows, then put crushed vitriol in place, and hold it there for an hour until the bleeding stops;
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	then return to your work until the stone is out, and have the instruments that I told you about in the extraction of stones for men to help you with your task;
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	and if the blood flows and it is an artery that has been cut, then put the powder on the wound and press hard with bandages and bindings, and do not stop pressing, and leave the stone and do not try to pull it out, for the patient might die;
puis cure la plaie.	then cure the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the swelling has gone down, return to your work so that the stone comes out.
de hernie carnouse	of a fleshy hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Ramice aquous is nothing other than an assembly of moisture or white albumen, which is beneath the shell of an egg.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	It is called "syfac", and sometimes it is found in the yolk of the egg, if one believes that it is another egg.
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	It is the skin of the egg between the white albumen that we have mentioned.
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	And this happens rarely.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this ramice is due to weakness that comes to the testicles and is spread out from there.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the eggs, and this moisture has many colours:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	or yellow, or colourless, or black, or watery white, and more besides.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And these are the signs to know this assembly, for if it is in the white albumen that we have mentioned, then the abscesses are small, as long as an egg, and do not pierce the shell, for there is moisture all around it.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the fabric itself, then the abscesses burst with an egg yolk, and because of this they think it is another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if the moisture is between the skin of the scrotum and the testicle, then he feels good;
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, examine all the way around, because the form is as described above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this, then, what comes after the insertion point, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we treat it with iron, then the patient should be bled according to his strength and the fullness of his body;
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	then have him lie on his back, on something slightly raised, and put a lot of bedding under him;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	then sit on his left, and instruct the assistant to sit on his right, and extend the scrotum towards one of the two sides of the heart;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	take the spatulate lead, and cut the skin of the scrotum from its base up to the testicle, and make the incision straight while slicing through the skin of the scrotum until you reach the white membrane, and carefully peel it away according to your ability.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	then pierce the testicle with a large needle and draw out all the water, then place your fingers in it, and it will rise again.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	and do not touch the heart of the testicle, but only the membrane.
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	cut it all around in sections, cutting the membrane carefully and not too deeply, for if you cut it badly, the water will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	and if the testicle bursts during your work, then reset it in its place when you have finished working on the membrane.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then stitch together the two lips of the heart of the testicle with one stitch, then treat it as you would any other wound until it heals.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	If you find that the egg is corrupted by another disease, then you should tie off the suspended vessels, fearing the flow of blood;
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	then cut open the scrotum throughout its suspension, and extract the testicle, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if pus has collected into two parts together, know that these are two sacs;
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	then cut open the other part in the same way you did the first, then wipe away the blood and put soft linen soaked in rosemary oil into the wound;
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and put another piece of soft linen soaked in wine and oil over the testicles, and place double layers of cloth over them, and tie it all together following this form:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two pieces of cloth and fill them with wool according to this shape and sew them together at the opening of the breeches, and one of the cloth pieces should reach from the anus to the back, and the other to the groin area;
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	and the other two on the two sides of the armpits, and all the restraint gathered at the buckle of the girdle;
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and sometimes medicine this ramification of cautery in place of the knife-edge of iron, and it is that you press the delicate knife, and cut the skin of the testicles, and it is heated as we have said, so that the white membrane containing the water is exposed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	if you take the cautery according to this form, and pierce that membrane gently, and scorch it with this delicate hot cautery;
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And scrape it in all ways that you can, until you draw out everything;
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and be careful that the fire does not touch the testicle;
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and know that this operation is much safer;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and must guard against bleeding and the wounds of cutting;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if anything opposes you, whether an abscess, or bloodletting, or something else, then cure what opposes you, according to what has already been said.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this procedure due to its horribleness, then use perforation as I have told you, and when you are certain by the signs we have mentioned that the pus is gone, then let the patient sit on a high seat:
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	then pierce the abscess in the part below at the full width of the spatula, and insert the perforator deep into the body;
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	and make the hole wide so that all the pus can flow out;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then put cotton on the wound, and tie it, and let the remainder of the pus drain, then treat the wound until it is healed;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	and if the white membrane does not let the pus out through the mouth of the wound, then you must push a feather or the instrument used to treat the water in hydrops into the wound, as described earlier;
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And the wound will open more widely and you will know that the fluid is returning, and it will come together after six months or around there, and when it has come together as before, thus the illness will pass its course.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicle abscess
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	You should know that in the dissection of this nerve there is fear of many dispositions, because of which I think it is better to leave it alone:
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	and I will tell you the work and the appearances of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	Therefore I say that many abscesses come in the body, and especially in the genitals;
et c’est par mout de cas.	and this is for many reasons.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	This is to know by an excess of sharp and bitter humor, which is spread in the genitals, or from a blow;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	and the color of the abscess according to the color of the body;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and does not cease to be painful, and is a serious abscess;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and sometimes there is an abscess grey and purulent and puss-filled, and sometimes it comes from a vein, or swelling of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is from a vein, it is recognizable by the hot nature of the abscess when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and you must not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	That which is from swelling of a vein is recognizable by its appearance when touched, and one can well make an incision on this type of abscess, and others like it;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	and you should cut the skin of the testicles, then the yolk will rise to the top, and the white part will become solid, and it will release the suspensory ligament from all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the yolk is already soured with these new characters, then you should cut open the egg and scrape it out;
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	and if it is on the skin or within the vessels, you must release all that tension and smooth out the lump.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the crack is at the back of the shell, then you must crack it all and extract the egg as we have said.Et s’il y a u neuue char ou dedens la tenve, si covient que tu la cope et la delivre, et mets l’uef en autre vaissel.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is done, then dress the wound with soft wool soaked in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other treatments until it heals.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicle abscess
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess wrapped in a wrapper like a berry, with the softening of the testicles, and it makes the patient very sick when he goes.
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	and the treatment of this disease is just as fearful as the one above, and yet we will still describe its treatment according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	You must make the patient sit on an elevated seat, then put the suspensory of the testicles down to your fingers, all along the vessels that are closest to the penis, and squeeze them firmly, and stretch them out;
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	then incise widely with a sharp spatula across the vessels, so that they are exposed, and then scrape from each side, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries that are in the temples;
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	then thread a needle with double thread, and tie it to the first place where the wire came out, and tie it directly to the other end.
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	then cut away at the skin evenly, according to the length of the body, and draw out the corrupted moisture.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	then treat the wound as in other wounds, so that no blood vessels are cut that nourish one of the testicles.
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	for there is no harm in this, and if the wire comes out through all the blood vessels, then the testicles must be pulled out of all the blood vessels.
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	so that the artery does not lose its nourishment due to the cutting of the blood vessels, and dry up and can no longer help itself.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rotgut wound
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The causes of this dislocation are due to the incision that comes from the armpit or the extension over the belly in the part of the inguinal canal, causing the intestines to descend from that opening to one of the testicles.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	and this dislocation occurs in the socket or from its extension, and these two methods come from many causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	or from impact, or from jumping, or from crying, or from lifting a heavy load, and through similar things;
