et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs that it is from the extension of the socket, are that it happens little by little over a long time, and does not occur suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscesses are even throughout, towards the depth, because the socket presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are when it is of the section of the sinus, that it causes sudden pain at the beginning, and there are different abscesses appearing underneath the skin close to the surface, and it is due to the discharge of the intestines and the body from the sinus.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the fester comes with the intestines, and is retained inside, and causes great suffering to the patient, especially when it is pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these treatments using iron, there is fear, which is why one should avoid them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the method of treatment is that you instruct the patient to push the intestines back into the wound with his hand, if he can;
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then hold his neck between your hands and lift his hips;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then lean the chest upwards, and cut all the skin of the long bones;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then insert hooks into the sides of the incision according to what you need to open the wound, and let it be such that the pus can come out.
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then scrape off the scurf that is under the skin of the scrotum, until the hard white scurf is uncovered all over.
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	then insert your index finger into the scrotum, between the white scurf that is under the skin of the testicle and between the second scurf, and separate what is behind the testicle and between the second scurf.
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and then move your right hand into the scrotum, and have the white scurf facing up towards your left hand, and lift the testicle out of all the scurf towards the incision.
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and instruct the assistant to extend the testicle upwards, and loosen what is tight behind the scrotum;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and examine with your fingers if he has any hard, white, membrane-like object in his intestines, and if you find anything, push it back down into the abdomen below.
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	Then take a needle with a thick thread made of six fibers, and insert it into the rear part of the membrane which is behind the scrotum's skin.
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	After threading the needle, pull the thread through the foreskin, leaving about twelve fibers exposed.
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	Then tie the fibers together in a cross shape and use it to tie the membrane, which we mentioned is under the scrotum's skin, with a strong knot of two parts.
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	Then wrap the threads around the testicles and tie them securely with a knot of two parts, ensuring that no blood vessels that supply them can pass through, so that no abscess forms.
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and put the plaster according to the first long line of two parts of this, and after these two lines let the syphon which is under the heart of the testicles be the larger part of an egg;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and after all the rest according to the roundness that the egg carries;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then cup in the part which is under the skin of the testicles, as much as the blood flows, and the bowels, as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then bring soft wool moistened in oil, and put it on the wounds, and then bring the plaster that we have described.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white syphilis that we have described is cauterized after the incision, due to doubt about blood flow.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this happens many times, and let the plaster hold until it bites through it;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it takes a long time to bite through, then be anointed with warm water, and put on what we have said, until it bites through;
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with other treatments, until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	of a fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I have never seen anyone dare to perform the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is done like the thread which is together with the screw, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after the incision slightly above or below.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	then press on it, and treat the abscess of the one who operates, until the vessels leak;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes a rupture occurs in the intestines, as we have said, and the orifice opens;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and none of the intestines come out through it, and if any do, it is a little, and it is repaired every hour;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and nevertheless, if he stays too long in this state, the wound putrefies and suppurates, so that the intestines protrude;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens because of the extension of the pus which is in the intestines, as we have said, for it is extended, then softened and swollen, and the orifice opens;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the treatment if by cautery, as we have said before;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and sometimes it is treated with iron in this way:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and the patient lies on his back between your hands, then apply the cautery to the root of the wart according to its size, three times;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	and then extract the skin tag underneath the skin, and then take the hair and place it on the visible spot where the tag was;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and press it firmly into the belly button, then cut the two visible spots on the hair shaft where the tag was, and cut both of them;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then pull out the hair shaft, and do not touch the skin tag or spread anything on it, as I have instructed you in the treatment for intestinal worms;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	then treat it like a wound.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, it cleans and cures the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	Syrup is constricting and has no appearance in the wound, and cautery is better for this purpose and closer to safety.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Many times the skin of testicles becomes soft in some men because the organs inside are softened and it is noticeable to look at.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	And when one wants to cure it, one should make the patient lie on his back, and press the soft skin on top of the natural skin;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	Then bring together the two lips with one stitch, and if you see it, sew the excess of the soft skin firmly with three or four stitches.
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Then press between the stitches, and heal it like other wounds until it is healed, and remove the thread.
dou chastrement	of chastisement
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	You should know that castration is considered a sin in our law, and because of this, I would prefer not to discuss it in this book.
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	It is only necessary for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	The first is that surgeons know how to respond when asked, and they know how to treat it.
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the others, because we often have need of the castration of certain beasts to help us, such as of a ram and a ewe and a kid and other animals.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say then that there are two types of castration:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	either by pulling or by cutting.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the type of castration that we perform by pulling, we make the animal sit in warm water so that the testicles are softened and dangling;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then grab them with your hand, until they are dislodged and you no longer feel them.Et la beste soit contrainct a demourer en aigue si longuement, tant qu’il soit asseré par la cuiture
Du chastrement de taille:	Of the castration by cutting:Car il faut que tu sache, que a nul
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	You should know that you must tie the scrotum with your left hand and press the skin of the testicles, then cut through both at once, when you have well-scalded them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and let some pus remain under the skin, and the subtle pus which is beneath the vessels.
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this method of castration is better than that which is done by pulling, because with the pulling some testicle might remain, causing the beast to desire sex.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then heal the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	There are two types of hermaphrodites in men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one is where between the two testicles there appears as much as the shape of a woman's nature, and it has hair, and sometimes it urinated standing up.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other method is for women, and it has on the buttock a rod-like protuberance and two testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment for both men and women is that you cut open the scrotum all around, and treat it as you would other wounds:
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	In the second type of hermaphrodite, men whose urine exits through the skin of the testicles require no treatment.
de la tentigene	of the testicles
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	A pustule is an unsightly swelling on the natural part.
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	And some women have them as large as a hand, and that is the cure.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	You should smear the excess of the pustule with your hand or a knife, and then cut it lightly;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not cut too deeply so that bleeding occurs, but cure the pustule with another cure until it is healed;
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and apply an ointment to another wound that arises at the mouth of the pustule; and perhaps it will burst, and is similar in appearance to a boil, and for this reason the ancients called it the 'cow disease'.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you must treat it, as we have said, with cautery, and heal it until it is cured.
de erratique	of erratics
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	It is erratic when the nature of the woman is not perceived, or the opening is small; and if the pustule bursts and the blood flows out, it is cured by another cure until it is healed.
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and is natural at birth, or accidental due to illness;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is caused by a wound, or by a subtle or dense toxin, and is made deep in the head, or in the sides, or below, or wherever it may be;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and conception, and childbirth, and perhaps flowers to have;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and the knowledge of the stars is through the observation of their paths.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the tumors are visible nearby, then use your fingers or a probe.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is so subtle that it approaches the two books, then you will hasten and they will surround him thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Place your two index fingers together, and let the woman be on her back with her legs spread;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	Then the two books are formed, so that the subtle star is surrounded, and the spell is cast over him;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	Then take wool, wet it in oil, and place it on the spot, and let the woman lie at home every day, so that she may not sweat.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the ulcer is hard and thick, then you must cut it with a spatulum like a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the spell is for a male child, then they suspend it on an ox and a he-goat;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	And have stanching medicines, such as agrimony, dragon's blood, incense, together with egg white;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	then administer a wide leaden cane, so that the wound does not heal closed;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and thus it remains for a long time, and then a tent of dry linen is administered;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then it is cleaned with other cleansings until it is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when there is fresh blood in a wound, it must be covered in this way, unless it is an abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For one must not cut into an abscess that is in the breast.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins from which blood flows without a break in the habit, and when hemorrhoids are old they become thrombosed;
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	And we have said in the division of similarities of us, and the signs, and I will say here those that receive cure.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and thrombosed external hemorrhoids, when they are perfectly formed in the anus and do not appear on examination, are not cured by iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those which are at the mouth of the anus, one can feel; these can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	Therefore, you should put the woman in a cold room, then the uterus is held with tweezers, and the neck in its roots, then powder is applied to medicines that restrict blood flow, such as acacia and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things;
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	then pour water over her feet for an hour, then put her in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	And if there is bleeding, let her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate peel and gall and similar things, then take barley flour, cook it with honey and garlic, and apply the ointment to her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it is stopped up, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, make her breathe through straws on her back and breasts without piercing;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	Then take wool, soak it in plantain juice or dogwood juice mixed with old wine, and breathe through it in the affected area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess has drained, treat the wound with ointment until it heals;
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and that which is called “albathir” is red and looks like rough felt, so it should be covered as I have said;
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then treat it until it heals.
des apostemes de la marris	Here is the translation of the text into English:
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many types of abscesses arise in the body, such as sores and pus-filled abscesses and herpes and boil and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscesses, and many other diseases that I have described in the classification.Et li apotomes de fevre sont plusors: or l’un est de la fleme; or l’autre est de sang; or l’autre est de sang et de fleme.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	Therefore, I shall describe in this treatise the hot abscess that occurs in the brain, which is not one of those that form in the bowels;S’il vient sus le chevel, si lo fai couper sus la tete, et li fai un bouton d’or fin ou de fer, et li leu estrainne les senges qui vienne a l’aposteme.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you wish to know the treatment with iron, look at whether the abscess is painful at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and whether it turns red if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Therefore, do not hurry to pierce it, but let it fester until the pain is relieved;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	then make the patient sit on a low stool or chair, with his legs bent and feet supported, leaning forward onto his knees;
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	let his thighs be spread apart, and let him place his arms under his knees, and tie them there well with a good bandage;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	then open the wound towards his right side, and insert the instrument to form the mouth of the wound, from which the pus will flow out afterwards;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and you must insert the instrument a little way in order to test the depth of the wound, so that when you insert the instrument further, it does not go in deeper than necessary and harm the patient;
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instruments are larger, then one must cover the depth of the wound with cloth so that the instruments do not cause pain;
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	one should put the point of the instrument at the top and hold it tightly.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when an abscess has been opened and one feels around in the wound with the hand, then one should cover the opening with a bandage, a sponge, or a cloth;
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the bowels are emptied, one should put into the wound moist tents soaked in rose oil, or in dried green oil;
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and put the tent above the wound at the bottom of the wound, and put over it a bandage and over that a clean lamb's wool soaked in water or mallows that have been cooked;
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then, after two days of treatment, until it is healed;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and sometimes we raise it and the wound with a clyster of water and honey, then of water or cooked roots of iris and arisarum.
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then return to the ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is closed in the wound, then you should guard against cooking with iron, but cure it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is necessary for the midwife to know the natural shape of childbirth and its signs; when you see the woman pushing downward and desiring to smell the ar:
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then the child hastens to come out;
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then you know that this childbirth is following nature's course, and the afterbirth comes out with the child;
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, you should gently press her belly so that the child comes out quickly;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	because when he emerges head-first, the afterbirth comes with him, and the birth canal is cleansed of its excess fluids through good cleansing;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and what comes otherwise does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For it sometimes comes under his feet, and comes out of his body or shoulder, and hands, or it comes on his stomach, or back, and is accidentally turned around his neck, and in other bad shapes;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	It is necessary for the surgeon to be wise and cunning in these things, and beware of error and deception, and I will show you all the shapes and how one should help them.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the infant comes out of its head by a natural opening, and the woman gives birth painfully, and her strength is weak, then make her sit on a saddle, or have women hold her;
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and place the الطبيب between their fingers the small spatula of which I spoke earlier:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and split the placenta, and scrape at its nail until the moisture that is inside flows out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and press the woman's abdomen so that the child comes down, and if it does not come down, then the woman must be enema with a mustard poultice with oil of six herbs;
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	then have her pressed and sneezing with a condiment, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	if the child does not come out right away.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if both hands are born first, then you must gently reset them little by little:
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot go in, put the woman on a chair, and lift her feet up;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then tip the chair back onto the ground, and hold the woman upright so that she does not slump forward;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and if the hands cannot go in and the child is dead, cut the hands at the joint which was described earlier, take out the child, and reset it in the same way.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	of the child's feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the infant comes onto its feet, it must be pushed upright.
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	And then rock it back and forth until it is steady.
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	Then grip one of its feet and stretch it out gently.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	Let the child jump up to its armpits, instruct it to grab hold, and then make it sneeze forcefully.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	If it jumps, God willing.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not jump out as we have said, then pull it back and forth gently until it is in its natural position.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it will be easy.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not jump as we desire, take mustard seeds, and six-year-old oil, and melted gum, and grind them all in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and apply this ointment to the woman's genitals, then make her sit in warm water up to her ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is soft underneath, put a myrrh collar on her and let it sit for an hour.
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then have her sit on a chair, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and lightly press her belly, for the child will jump now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	from the birth of the child on his knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this way, he puts his hands on it bit by bit.
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then she should lie on her back, and her feet hang down, and she should lie on the bed.
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and fold her hands bit by bit, and then she presses her hands on her belly, and takes the cushions from under her, so that she is aligned downward.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not jump, take her feet and move them around, then move her belly upward, then press with your hands.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and rock the child bit by bit.
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and instruct the woman to press until the child emerges.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	of the child's exit, which comes out as wide as a hand
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	You should trick your hand into emerging:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if it cannot be returned, then have the woman walk and stand.
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot walk, then have her lie on her bed and lift her legs straight up;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then bring the mustard plaster that I mentioned earlier;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, then have her sit on a chair and study how to return the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and bring out the child according to its natural shape, and have her sneeze, and command that she hold on until the baby comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	from the baby's exit on its neck, and have her hands spread out, and her face turned towards her mother's back
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	I should grip her hand, then push it little by little, and move it gently;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is even, put on the mustard plaster of vinegar and oil, as we said, then command that she move little by little;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done this, have her sit on a chair, and command that she holds on;
et la fai esternuer.	and let it sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same way for all of the afterbirth
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When all the secondina comes out in this way, then grip the secondina with your nail until the moisture is released;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the infant vomits on its face and neck, grip it by the head until the moisture is released and the infant dies;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then put the infant back inside, so that it is positioned correctly, and instruct the woman to grip herself a few times:
adonques si istra legierement.	then she will be delivered easily.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the issue of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that twins are born many times, and sometimes three or four are born;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not a strange thing, but it happens rarely.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	They are strange, and do not live long if they are;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they are multiplied, and are separated by the placenta, which is attached to the womb;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they emerge as naturally as a tooth, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they emerge painfully, then the surgeon should follow our instructions, and be subtle, quick, and light-handed in what he does.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and thus act as he sees fit for their health.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the womb in one, two, three, four, five, six or seven, or more to fifteen, and they are all formed like children in the measure of the glorious sage, and the surgeon should know all this, because sometimes similar things happen.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	then he should act according to what is appropriate.Et s’il avient que il ait en la marris uns ou plusors qui ne se
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you are treating a woman for a dead child or an abdomen, as I have said in the section on obstetrics, and there is no movement, and you are forced to use your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	then you must know if the woman is of sound mind, and has no accident where she has fear of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	then the woman should be laid on her back, with her hips tilted down, and her legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the midwife should apply the herbal remedy to the perineum if she is tied to the bed so that she does not drop the baby;si la femme est sovinee sus ses deux chiés, et li ministre lui teigne la vouture entre les deux jambes;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then the woman is laid on her two hips, and the midwife applies the herbal remedy to the perineum between the two legs; then rub the mouth of the mother with moist oils mixed with mustard seed and fenugreek and linseed, then anoint the midwife's hands with these oils and herbs;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	then they are put into the mother gently, then they examine where she feels the pinching that is suitable for this, and take care if the child is positioned to descend on its head;si la marris ne senton point la dislocation des chiés qu’il faille le chié droit ou le gauche, puis les bouton en legierement ou il faille, si la marris senton li enfes apparilliez a dessendre, s’il est legierement apparilliez, si doit il estre dessendue
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	if they put the weasels on their eyes, or in their throat, mouth, palette, under their beard, in their armpit, or near their ribs, and if the swelling is on the feet, they should be placed on the feet, and on the sides.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and it is necessary to hold the weasel in their right hand, and place the cloth between their left fingers, and tie it around their whole hand lightly, then insert the weasel into any of the places that we have mentioned, until it reaches the hollow.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is how to prepare the weasel:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then place another weasel against it, or one-third of the size if you need more, so that the extractions are equal.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	then they are pressed equally from both sides, to push out, and the weasels are held in place with teeth, like this:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if any part of it remains, then anoint one of his fingers with oil, and rub it in that part, and draw out the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if nothing remains, then place this incision higher up, and do this until it all comes out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other, and it cannot be returned due to the tightness, then you must wrap a cloth around it, until it all comes out;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	then apply the cupping in the bend of the wrist or at the elbow, and so you must do for the other hand, and also for the feet.Et si il demoure ainscun sang, si le mets sus I drapeil, et le tiens tant qu’il fuie tout;
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if any blood remains, then place it on the cloth and hold it until it all comes out; And if the head of the child is large and it is tight in the birth canal, or if there is a gathering of pus at the head, then you must insert the spiny spatum between your fingers, pierce the head, and draw out the pus;
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or to use the instrument called "almidach", from which the form comes with the instruments or chapter that follows this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and thus the same way, make if the child has a large head naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull out the bones with tongs, and if the head jumps out and is forced, let it be broken, until the moisture that is in the wound comes out;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, then cut it in pieces to the extent that you can;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen on the belly or under the ribs, then you must pierce it so that the moisture runs out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is above his feet, the pulse is light, and the breath comes easily to the mouth.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is constricted in the belly or the foot, then you must stretch it with your hand wrapped in a cloth;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and cut open the belly or the foot so that the moisture that is inside comes out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other limbs are paralyzed, and the neck remains, then he puts his hand into the wound up to the mouth of the wound;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then he puts in a hook or two, and pulls it out;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the wound is constricted by a hot abscess that has come to it, then one should not work on it, but apply moist and fatty substances;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and he applies poultices, and uses warm moistening fluids.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the testicle is on his side, and you can make it even, then apply what we have said about a living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one has no power over it, he pulls it out in pieces, leaving nothing of the testicle behind.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, apply what we have said about hot abscesses that come to the wound;et s’il vient de lassitude ou de fraicheur, si amenistre choses froides et molifians.
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if blood flows, let it be placed in a water restraint, and administer other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman whose fetus had died within her; then another was sewn over him, and the other died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time an abscess came in his arm, and swelled so much that it opened, and began to discharge profusely.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the priest, and I thought long and hard, but could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a strong drawing plaster, and out came a bone, and after a few days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very amazed, because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought that they were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I wanted to see the wound, and as soon as I laid hands on it, the woman felt better.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and the woman lived for a long time like that, and then she suddenly died.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	And I haven't mentioned this chapter before because when masters find something strange, they know how to treat it.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to return the dislocated shoulder to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Now we come to the form of pressure which is found in books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and in the second turn, at the head of the second line.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, the horns should be more subtle and made of ivory or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth of the tube should be two fingers wide and the rim of the trees one and a half palms long;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and let the two limbs be made of the same wood, which are firmly joined together at one end and separated by half a palm's width or slightly more at the other.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two extensions are fitted into the mouth of the wound to open it when the two horns are turned.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	A more subtle and lightweight form is made of boxwood or ebony, according to the appearance of tongs;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and has two extensions, as you see, a palm long and two digits wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see the wound open to all the instrument, then let the woman lie on her bed, with her feet hanging and her legs open, then insert the two extensions together into the wound, and hold the head of the instrument between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand into the instrument, just as you did with the tongs, depending on how much you want to open the mouth of the wound, until the patient does what she wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	This instrument is completely decorated and has many variations in its appearance.
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when the patient sees them prepared, the operation is faster and more skilled for their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despair over the instrument, but prepare it, for their need is inexcusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you should instruct the patient to hold back her breath, then make her sneeze gently, and then squeeze her mouth and nose tightly;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she vomits, all the better.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a pot and place herbs that can open the mouth of the wound inside, such as chamomile, anise, rue, camphor, and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	all these herbs, or any of them, are cooked in water over fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then put one end of the pipe into the pot and the other end into the mouth of the patient, and apply it until the vapors enter the patient's mouth;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then make the patient sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the pus comes out quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if she remains after this treatment and does not pass away, as we have said, command the midwife to wet her left hand in oil of assafety or in a poultice of alder, and then put it into the birth canal, and draw out the placenta;
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, she should grab it and stretch it little by little, straightening it out, so that the patient does not feel pain during extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but she must move it gently to the right and left, and then pull it out;
si venra et se desaerdra.	it will come and be released.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the wound is tight, we have described the cure for sneezing, and the fumigation of herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not cured by all that we have said, then be sure to follow the treatment;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that he who is at the mouth of the wound be tied to the thigh of the woman, then cleanse her with a four-fold ointment;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	if she expels and releases it, and comes out;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	but still, when she expels, a bad odour comes to the stomach and head, and the disease worsens.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Therefore, it is necessary to use suitable fumigations:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	some of the ancients have tried fumigation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The instrument used to fumigate the woman for retained placenta and afterbirth is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	It is like glass, and one puts the narrow end in the wound, and the wide end above the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and apply the fume to the coals, and to the lice until they are gone, then start another.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the fundament
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born without their foreskin pierced; instead, it is closed by a thin membrane.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	So the midwife should pierce this membrane with her finger nail and not cut it with a sharp instrument, and she should be careful not to tear it.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then put wet linen in wine and oil on the wound until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will heal, then put a wooden splint through the wound and leave it for several days, then remove it when the child wants to walk around.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this membrane comes from a wound or an abscess suddenly;
si covient coper celui soudement:	then cover it quickly:et s’ele est en la bouche, si le met sus lainne mouille
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	and if it is in the mouth, then wet linen should be applied and treated as we have said about the caustic of the stone.
de la fistule dou fondement	from the fistula of the fundament
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from under the foreskin are called nodations, and those that grow from beneath the foreskin, or in the space between the two parts, are either single or multiple.Et s’ele est en la bouche, si le met sus lainne mouille
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	and when this knot is old, it opens, and often emits moisture or pus, and sometimes these ulcers are persistent;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and they are caused when there is flatulence or vomiting, or sometimes a burst vessel.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if there are fistulas that pierce all the way to the bladder, and halfway down the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and they can reach all the way to the hip joint, and to the knee.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows a persistent fistula in the anus, and not a persistent one;
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you should thrust your index finger into the anus, and push a fine needle made of brass or iron into the fistula when there is no crookedness.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if there is crookedness, then push in a thin rod or horse hair until you feel the rod or hair with your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and it does not come out through the anus as flatulence or wind, nor turn green, as we have said;
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	you know that it has not pierced through;
si te haste dou curer.	then cure it quickly.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula penetrates as far as the bladder or the duct of urine, and urine escapes, and cannot be stopped by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced just up to the hip joint, then the vein is flowing just up to that spot;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is a twisting and the pain spreads around, then it has entered there, and neither medicine nor poultices help;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these piercing sores there is no cure except through hard work, and the foolishness of those who meddle is useless.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In the one that is not pierced and is not old, there is hope of healing by fire, as I have proven, and the patient lies between your hands on his back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and he will raise his legs up to his thighs, and have his thighs inclined towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then insert a tent of copper or lead, if there is any tortuosity that you know about, where the tent should go.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If he feels pain in his anus, then you must insert your index finger if the tent has not pierced him;
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and where you feel the anus or the flesh, then you know that it is pierced;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if they cannot work on it, then it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	They say that some can still be healed, but that rarely happens;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the treatment that is given, they scorch the wound with a subtle cautery according to the size of the fistula, as it was previously stated;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and insert it fully into the fistula until it comes out from the anus;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two or three times until you know that these false hairs are singed, which resemble an owl's feather.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	then dress the wound with wet bandages in butter until these hairs come out, then dress the wound with ointment binding the hair and sealing it.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If he is healed in this way, it is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this does not work, he cannot be healed otherwise;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent pierces and does not reach the bone which is in the foundation, and there is between your finger and the tent a thick covering of hair or of syphac, and you see the fistula following the covering to the core;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if the tent is pulled at the beginning of the fistula and pushed in before the tent, and then cauterized afterwards until it reaches the tip of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the tent will be delivered and will fall out;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then defecate those charred bones that look like bird feathers, and leave nothing behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the pus comes out and flows between you and the wound, then cauterize it with fire or with an astringent medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For fire cautery draws together two bone things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the burning of those charred bones, and the clotting of blood and the drying up of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then the treatment of moist tents with butter or crushed things, until the bowels move, and let the burnt bones leave the body;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound of hard, dry, burning lumps, and the remedies are dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes all the way to the bottom of the foundation, and is removed from the body, put your finger or foundation in it, and inquire about it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the bowels, and there is a lump of pus or char in it, about to burst, then there is no hope except through faith and hope, by administering one of three remedies:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	either you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut into it to the depth, or if you can, put in tents and treat it as before;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deeply, lest you pierce the organ that holds the foundation, and cause the evacuations to emerge unwillingly through that channel;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance, you may be healed by removing that covering and cleaning it after the wound has been exposed, either with a tent or another sharp instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then cut away at the diseased flesh within the wound as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	then strive to close the wound and stop the fistula from spreading in the region above the foundation:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	if it is more beneficial for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes they are like this:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and when you insert the tent into the fistula, and it is near the foundation beneath the skin, take a tent pierced at its tip in this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And he inserts a twisted thread into it, and he inserts the tent along the entire thread into the fistula until it reaches the tip.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is perceived at the edge of the foundation within, then pull out the thread from that hole, as you would press your finger into the fundament.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and pull the end of the thread, and bring the two heads together, and press them against each other, and leave it for one or two days.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it sometimes so that the threads catch those hairs that are between, and grow together.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then cure the wound until it is healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not open on its own, then you must make it open in every way that you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not appropriate to cover the wound with a bandage, then treat it, as we have said, until it has healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spatulon spine which they make for the fistula is very sharp and pointed on one side.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other side it is not, so that one does not catch what one should not, as you can see here.
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Hemorrhoids occur in two ways:L’une est de la cossine qui se part en cossine en
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	or they are within the anus, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and some produce blood, and there may be one or more, and they are located within and at the top of the anus.
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those that protrude have a little moisture, and sometimes pus or a little yellow water or blood, and they are the colour of the body.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment for those who have them within the anus is that you instruct the patient to straining until they go into a chamber, so that the anus opens and the warts are visible.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	then grab it with tweezers or your fingernail, then pull it out by its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the tweezers cannot hold them because of their moisture, then take them with a piece of cloth, or cotton, or a piece of camel hair;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and pull them with your fingers, then press and powder on some hot powders that are in place of cautery;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you can cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cautery, then treat them with other treatments until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the fundament cannot exit, then enema the patient with a harsh and asper enema to clean what is in the fundament so that it can exit clearly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	then the patient defecates, and if the thread comes out of the anus, then the treatment is light;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you should grab them with your fingernail or tweezers, and press, then treat as we have said, until it is healed and fears the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	You should administer the suturing in this way:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	take a twisted thread, and put it in a needle, and then draw the thread above and pierce the needle from the other side, and turn both ends of the thread under the needle, and let it be loose;
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and tighten the thread, then tie the thread, and remove the needle, and do likewise with all the others, and leave one to drain the excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place a moistened cloth in rose oil or cerate over the wound, and place it on the wound, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then let him stay until he defecates, and when it is passed, treat the wound with ointment and other remedies until it is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	from dryness of the anus or rectum
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Drying of the bowels occurs often in the intestines, due to constipation from natural causes, and when the disease is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	If necessary, cut the tip of a spatula or your fingernail to create a scrape that does not leave moisture behind;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then treat it until it is cured as it should be;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot heal, then restart the scraping more fiercely than before, until it heals a lot and is scalded;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it until it is healed.
dou fremit	where there is trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A wart is a small appearance formed under the body, and goes very deep;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes the frost bites it, and one feels it like dead from trembling, and it comes all over the body, and more in the hands than anywhere else.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And its cure is that you take a straw of an goose feather, or a strong vulture feather, and place the straw on the trembling, until the purple circle trembles all around it;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	then turn your hand to all of the straw until you scrape all around the trembling, and push it deeply in, and uproot the trembling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see fit, make a cane of bronze or iron according to this shape, and let it be thin underneath and drawn out on top:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	it does not pierce, so as to keep it in place, and to press tightly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see, if you cauterize the tremor, as it is before the cautery chapter.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes they make a clyster of silver or of brass, or of melted copper or alloyed;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	and sometimes they make these small and large instruments, according to those who have them.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those which are administered for the treatment of children and the weak and painful are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the small and large enema is above wide, or the belly is bound according to this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	and there is a deviation in the bellies, and the intestines are pierced inside, as you can see;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and on one side there are two openings, and on the other one;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and the belly where one puts medicines is made of a beast's bladder or parchment, and it is pierced all around with small openings, and there is about an inch between each opening, then insert into these openings a strong thread of twisted thread in the shape of X or entwined around, and assemble the belly so that it looks like a goat;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	and when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument with a strong thread, then administer a clyster.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and this is the form of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine be neither too hot nor too cold, and anoint the tip of the clyster with oil or egg white, or similar, then insert it gently;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	then the minister squeezes it with both hands together until it is empty, then removes the clyster and lets the patient lie on his side, and if the medicine wants to come out, he should press as hard as he can;
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if he sleeps for a night, it is even better.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you use the clistere for the disease of stomach ache, and the medicine rushes to come out, then repeat it until he is cured.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are in the anus or rectum, then the clyster should be as thin as for a child;
