et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the thin clyster that presses against the skin:
des plaies	Of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have already discussed the treatment of wounds in the previous section.
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	Now we will discuss the cures using hands and medicine, according to their effectiveness.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and by what they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The causes of wounds are due to the impact of stones, or cutting with a sword, knife, lance, spear, arrow, or similar objects.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	Wounds can occur in various parts of the body, such as the neck, head, leg, belly, liver, and other similar organs.
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	I will now discuss the treatment for each type of wound, starting with simple head wounds, as this will lead us to remember other related topics in this chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound occurs on the head, and the bone is not broken, you should first check if it was caused by the impact of a stone or similar object, and if the skin is still intact but the wound is large, and you suspect a hot abscess:
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	if he bleeds from the cephalic vein immediately, and there is little blood from the wound, and let the bleeding be in the opposite direction of the injured part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and prevent the patient from becoming bloated with wine and rich foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not want to bleed, then his food should be reduced, and he should not drink wine or eat meat;
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	and place cotton wet with rose oil only on the wound, if hot abscesses appear; or wine with a styptic;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	and if there is no hot abscess, then place on the wound, if it has all its blood and has not been moved by the air, a powder which I will describe shortly;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if it has been moved by heat, then place on it some ointments until it heals.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large, like that of a sword, and the lips cannot be brought together with tenting, then stitch them together, as I will describe for abdominal wounds.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	If the wound is exposed to the bone, and it can be seen, and it is not holding on except for a little bit, then cut it off.
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	then heal the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh in place of skin, and instruct the patient to eat coarse foods like testicles and cooked wheat, as well as meat, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find pus in the skin, and it is not reaching the bone, then cut off all the pus, and drain it out, then heal it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein, which causes bleeding that cannot be stopped by medicine, then tie it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if this does not help, then cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere:	And if these wounds are small and simple, then the cure is easy:
et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	and you shall put this powder on so that the burn has moved.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est:	And the manner of the powder is as follows:
pren encens une partie;	take frankincense one part;
sanc de dragon II parties;	dragon's blood two parts;
chalz vive III parties, et le poudre subtilment, et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	burn the ingredients together and grind them into a fine powder, then apply it to the wound, pressing it firmly so that it sticks well and draws out all the blood;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle;	then bind it tightly, leaving it in place until the swelling goes down;
car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	and one does not remove the medicine until the wound is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes one does this with chalk alone, when one doesn't have incense or dragon's blood, but that the wound is moved by the fire.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the burn has moved the wound, simply leave it as it is, without applying any of the powder;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but apply some digestive poultices made from barley flour and water or honey, until the wound drains well;
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat other wounds until he is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the fracture of the bone comes with the wound, and it is small, then extract it with fine tweezers:
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about fractures of the head next.
de la plaie dou col	of the wound on the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If a wound occurs on the neck and it is single, then there is no difference between it and one in the head, but if the nerve of the neck or artery is cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is a nerve, do not treat the wound, and do not apply anything constricting, because it harms nerves and makes them retract;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	and put nothing cold on the wound, for the substance of the nerves is cold, and their continuance is with the brain, which is the highest member;
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce, et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	but let the medicine be warm, as with warm water washed chalk, and mixed with rose oil, and cuce washed also in warm water, and other minerals of the same kind, and moist ointments.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, then cut and bind it, then treat it until it heals.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and there is pus and swelling, then pierce them higher up;
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	and if an artery is cut, and there is bleeding, then ligature it, and stop it, and cauterize it if necessary;
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va, si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	and if the spine of the throat is cut, or the windpipe, and the passageway for food is blocked, then cut open the neck above the Adam's Apple, and do not touch the throat but reset it according to its natural shape;
et puis l’estraint avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then hold it gently, and leave it for several days, then treat with ointments that promote healing until it is healed;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound has left an impression on the bone, then treat it thus:
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse, et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	and if there are bone fragments, remove them all if you can, and those that you cannot reach, leave them until the wound suppurates, is cleaned out, and the passage is cleared;
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	and if the wound is fresh, apply the powder I have described above.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and there is a fistula, treat it as I have said in that chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the wound of a spear or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne:	If it is a deep wound from a lance or knife, and the patient is not vomiting wind, then:
saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	you will know that the wound is mortal;et si tu ves que la chair est verte ou noire, ou qu’il y ait sanguine en la chair
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont, et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and if the wound is not deep and is fresh with all its blood, then do not apply the powder at first, nor ligature it for fear of the blood clottings breaking loose, returning to the heart, and killing the patient;et si li sang ne demort pas em parfond, et n’est pas venimeux, et la chair n’est noire ne verte, et le sang n’y est, si n’a grant dolor, si le laisse au repos et a leu de sang qui vienne, et le guarisira;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie II fois le jor;	but I apply an attractive ointment, and bind it twice a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor, et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie III jors, ou IIII, ou plusors;	and if you don't have ointment, put old cotton in the wound to draw out moisture, and let the patient sleep with their head on the wound for three, four or more days;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’estraingnemens d’alainne;	and if there is no spasming, nor trembling of the heart, nor strangulation of the throat;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see these good signs, you will know that the wound is saved.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Heal it then with poultices and other remedies until it is healed;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule;	and if it cannot heal, and there is still discharge, then you will know that there is a fistula;
si la cure si com on doit.	treat it then as one should.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife, and it is superficial, or deep, or in the back, then treat it as described above;
s’elle est grans, de cousture;	if it is large, with stitching;
et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	and if it is small, with powder, and if it is pressed into the bone, and has torn away pieces, then the wound, and the bones are displaced if they are dislocated;
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not dislocated, then let the wound fester, so as to lessen the extractions;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	and for other wounds in other limbs, the judgment is as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	from a rupture of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	Breaking of the belly occurs in large, medium and small ways;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	of the great wound sometimes the intestines, or the nerves of the intestines, by which the entry of air;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans, por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	and stitching is more difficult, and sometimes the small wound is worse than the large one, because one puts the intestines back in more with pins, if they are not put back gently from hot to cold;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes, et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres II.	because the intestines swell as soon as they feel the cold, they contract more at their tips, and due to this, the wound heals better, so one must reset the intestines to their place, rather than the others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc IIII manieres:	And you should know that there are three types of hernia in the abdomen:
les II costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre, et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et II autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	The two common hernias occur in the abdominal wall, and the hernias of other wounds in the body, and there are two other types of hernia that are specific to certain wounds.
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	Nevertheless, they are more common with abdominal walls, and I will describe each one and make it clear.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer, et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des II manieres:	I say that when the wound is small, and a little bit of intestine has come out, and it can be easily put back in, then it is one of two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit, ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	either because the wound is small, as we have said, or because the intestines are swollen due to cold.Et a ceste costure covient il que tu mues les intestins a son lieu et qu’il ne se demourent en l’enduit ou li plaie est fait.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, heat it in such a way:
moillie une esponge ou I mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement, ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique, et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	wet a sponge or a soft cloth in warm water only, or cook it in squint water and cypress and spike and rose until the swelling is relieved;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	and sometimes this wine is restraining, and it is used alone to reduce swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites, car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	And when you see the swelling leaving, then moisten the intestine with water or old wine in which are cooked mallows and marjoram, for by this the entrance is made easier for a little while.
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, then make a small cut in the instrument with which they cut hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille, que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	and the first cure is made to the wound, from which one must not cut without great necessity;si li taille est saine de l’entree sus la plaie, et quonque ne muoie, si convien la curiere dousement a l’enfeure que
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the instrument to split it with:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut inside at an angle and do not go straight through, and look here at the shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer, si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre, se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestines jump out, then put them back according to their natural shape in their proper place, if you have the power, for this is better.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre, si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	When the wound is large, and it is in the lower part of the belly, then you must have the patient lie on his back with his legs higher than his head:
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre, si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz, et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des II parties si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	and if it is in the lower part of the belly, then put the head and feet higher than the lower parts, and also if the rupture of the belly is in one of the two sides, then have the patient turn onto that side so that the wounded part is higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and thus you must conduct yourself with large and small wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet, puis aies entre tes mains I ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main, et assemble les levres;	With small wounds, take what you have ready, then grip with your fingers the edges of the wound all around, and bring them together;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures, et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie, puis laisse des le chief de la plaie I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait I boin fil fort;	and this is the common way of stitching, and it is that you take a needle or more, according to the width of the wound, then leave from the head of the wound two threads' worth of space, and thread a needle with a strong thread through it;
et perce les II chiés dou cuir avec les II chiés dou siphac, qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie, et assemble les II chief dou siphac les IIII ensamble;	and pierce the two sides of the skin with the two sides of the sutures, which is underneath the skin inside, so that you make it pierce from that part, and tie the two ends of the sutures together;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de II pars, puis assemble les II chiés de la plaie avenanment, et puis laisse I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	then draw the thread through twice around the needle from both sides, then bring the two sides of the wound together evenly, and then leave two threads' worth of space, and thread another needle;et ainsi tu faices II ou IIII couppes selonc la quantiteit de la plaie.
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille, et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles, tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	and tie the thread as you did with the first needle, and do not cease to do so according to your need for needles, until the entire wound is bound;et si il advient qu’il ne se peust restrainer avec les aguilles, mais aine qu’on le poisse destrer, il covient que l’on le destreive, et que l’on lie les chiés dou cuir entor la plaie selonc la maniere
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses, car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	let the needles be medium-sized, both fine and thick, for fine needles cut through all flesh, and very thick ones cannot enter well.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	because of this they should be medium-sized.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir, k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	and one must not push the needles too deep into the flesh and through the skin so that they do not cut and open the wound before the wound is closed.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir, et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir, et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	then one should cover the heads of the needles so that they do not hurt the patient when he sleeps, and put tents or bandages over the heads of the needles to keep them in place, and leave them until the wound is closed.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies, car il i soffist une aguille ou II.	and this method of stitching with needles is most suitable for small wounds, because only one or two needles are needed.Et quant li malaide a grant plaie, si convient qu’il soit costé a la manière de l’esguile; et puis li covient mettre le drapelz ou la tente sus li pi
Li seconde costure si est commune, et est que tu assemble les II chiés dou cuir et les II chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait I fort fil moien;	The second stitch is common and is where you bring together the two ends of the skin and the two ends of the הסית (syt, a type of cloth) with a needle and strong thread.
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz IIII ensamble, si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	And when you have pierced all four ends together, bring the needle back to the place where you started, in the way that one sews a dress.
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	And space each stitch with the thickness of a little finger.
ceste costure sevent li home, et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre, qui estoit navrez d’un coutel, et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant, et issoit des intestines bien II palmes de grant, et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	This stitch is good for a man, and I sewed up a wound that a man had on his belly, which was cut with a knife, and the wound was more than a palm wide, and the intestines were exposed for more than two palms in width, and the wound was in the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit XXIIII houres fuer, et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a XV jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	I brought him back to health after his intestine had been outside for 24 hours, and the wound was sewn up for 15 days, and I treated it, and he recovered.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they thought he would die, and it was a miracle:
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en I leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and I did not treat him with ointment, because I was in a place where none could be found, nor any medicine;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel II fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and apply cotton wool soaked in honey to the wound twice a day, and wash it with water until it is healed.
Or vos dirai les II propres manieres de cousture:	Or I shall tell thee of two proper ways of suturing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	take the needle and insert it in the wound from the outside just until it touches the interior;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille, et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	when it has pierced the skin straight through, then hold the eye of the needle where it entered and pull it through from the inside out until it emerges on the outside;
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz, et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and the technique of this suturing is that you sew as the furriers sew furs, leaving some skin on one side and taking some from the other, so that the sutures are completed.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement, si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les II parties ensamble naturelment, et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	The second method of suturing which Galen describes correctly, is done as some people join two pieces of skin naturally and apply one edge of the wound to the other, thus:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement, et laisse les II chiés dou syfac;	stick a needle or needle tip, and pierce that area only, and leave the two ears of the syringe;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, as II chiés dou syfac;	then turn the needle and pierce from the outside towards the inside, to the two ears of the syringe; and draw blood until it flows freely through both ears.
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en II autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then pierce one and then the other from the outside towards the inside, in two other ears of the syringe that are on the opposite side; and draw blood until it flows freely through both ears.
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and this is the usual method of suturing and the most common.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent, c’on doit coudre le ventre a II aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	Galen says this word, and some testify to it, that one should sew the belly with two needles, with thread in each; and when you have sewed both sides of the wound, pass the needle through from one side to the other, and then back again, so that the thread lies across the middle of the wound.
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and one should push one needle from one side and the other from the other, in the manner of those who sew sores; and when you have sewed both sides of the wound, pass the needle through from one side to the other, and then back again, so that the thread lies across the middle of the wound.and when you have sewed both sides of
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre, si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	and know that when the rupture is in the belly, then the cure is more difficult than from other places in the belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgment of the wound is such as the judgment of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee, si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout;	and it is so that when you find the fresh wound full of blood, as long as the wound has not bled, then put back the intestine and the gut;
puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char, et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	then put on healing powder, and if the wound has bled, then put on any suitable ointment until the wound heals over;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and tie the thread, and sew the lips of the wound, and the muscle;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat the wound as the others, until it is healed;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel, et le remue II fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and if you have no medicine, then put on old cotton, and change it twice a day until it is healed.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you need no other medicine in many situations where the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz, si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset, et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and if you doubt that the wound will affect the principal members, then you should wet a light woolen cloth in tempered oil or rose oil, and place it around the wounds, and under the armpits;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient, si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	and if there is pain or a swelling in the bowels, which often happens, then cleanse with a clyster of tepid black wine, especially if the swelling reaches the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	and pierce it from within, and know that when it is the large intestine, it is easier to heal than the small one.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez, et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	The intestines, which are called 'young', cannot heal when they are injured, and this is due to the thinness of the veins through which they run, and the subtlety of the entire body, and their close connection to the nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the membrane jumps out of the wound, then put it back in as the intestine, while it is still fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, car il i a voinnes et arteres;	and if it is old and become green or black, then you must tie off the area that is black so that bleeding vessels don't come, for there are veins and arteries there;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien, et met les II chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	then grasp what is between the ligaments, and place both heads dangling from the bottom part of the wound to loosen the extraction when the sutures are cut, and the wound heals.
de la routure dou boueil	of the route of the boil
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite, si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes, por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	When the intestines protrude and the wound is small, it can sometimes be healed in some people, because I saw a man who was stabbed in the belly;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac, et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	the wound was on the right side of the stomach, and it became a fistula, and from it came excrement and flatulence;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I applied treatment according to what I knew, and did not cease to treat him gently until he was healed and the wound closed.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw it healing, I feared that the man had discomfort in his belly;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	but there was no discomfort, and he stayed in good condition, eating and drinking;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	and some experimenters say that when there is a small wound in the intestines, it should be bound up in such a way:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie, et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les II levres, si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	take a piece of sheep's testicle, then bring together the lips of the wound, and when the testicle is unfurled, place it over both lips so that it holds them shut.
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier, puis met I autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	Then tie the testicle to the head, and it will stay in place so that it cannot be dislodged. Then put another testicle after it in the same way until the wound is completely bound up.
et cout la plaie.	And then dress the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide, et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste, en teil maniere:	If they are wounds in the intestines, and no harm comes to the patient, then one can ligate the intestines with a fine thread cut from an animal's intestine, in such a way:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez, et puis lie au chief de cest fil I fil de lin subtil tort, puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	take the end of this intestine thread which is very thin, and then tie to the end of this fine linen thread, put the thread through a needle, and sew up the intestines, and reset it in its proper place.Car il doit estre liiez l’intestine par le fil de lin, et li chief liier a l’intestine d’une beste si qu’il ne se puet desliier;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	and this method of sewing up the perineum is not appropriate except according to the way of faith and hope.
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	and if the wound is great and wide, especially when it is in one of the grave intestinal diseases, then there is no remedy or healing except with subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of fistula wherever it may be
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule», et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	Know that any wound or abscess, when it wakes up, is universally called a "fistula", and especially when it is hooded and bowed in.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor, et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	And a fistula is according to the verdant nodulation of a hard and white tumor, where one does not feel pain, and it is as common as the feather of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	and sometimes it is in a clear bowels, and sometimes dense;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	sometimes small, and sometimes enough;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char, ce n’est fuers que par une des VIIII causes:	and I have spoken of it in the division of wounds, that every wound that is not healed, and there is no flesh, it is not due to one of the VIII causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	that is, by the smallness of blood or body;
ou por sa malice;	or for his malice;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is a hard lump within it, and upon the lips, which prevents the growth of hair;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	or because he has too much bowels;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	or because the skin is shrivelled and the matter within is of poor quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or because the medicine is not good for the treatment;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because the putrefaction is of a pestilential nature;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	or because the digestion in the region is tardy and slow, and health is delayed, and there is swelling by nature;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	or because there are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	And I have already shown all these causes, and the signs, and the treatments with medicine in the division.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	Now I will tell you about the treatment for a fistula that is done with the hands.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	You should know that fistulas occur throughout the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners, ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes, ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	because they can come from large veins, or arteries, or nerves, or the eye, or the intestine, or the bladder, or any part of the sides, or the spine in the back, or any joint in the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and if it affects the principal part of the limb, and similar places.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all fistulas that are in this way are very painful to heal, and there is nothing but hard work and ignorance;
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure, et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	and if there is any fistula that does not reach the point I have described, and you are confident in the cure, and you see it working, then take a tent of iron or bronze, if the fistula is straight, and pierce it;
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc, car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	and if the fistula is crooked, then use a thin tent of lead, because lead bends around the curvature;
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes, si la clisterize par l’un des pertus, car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	and if the fistula has several openings and you cannot pierce it with tents, then cleanse it by cauterizing one of the openings, because moisture travels from one opening to another;
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont, et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	then pierce it as hard as you can, so that you may discover whether there is a bone or nerve, and whether it is deep, and ask the patient about their pain when you press your hand, and where they feel it;
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine, ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit, et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and when you know the true location of it, and whether it is near a joint or nerve or artery or vein, or in any of the places I have told you, then cut according to what I have instructed, and remove the diseased flesh and rotten bones within.
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee, et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues, puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule, tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	then treat the wound until it heals; and if the fistula is deep and in a good location, you should cut it deeply, as much as you can, then place moist tents in medicinal vinegar, and insert them into the fistula up to its head, so that the medicine corrodes the excess matter remaining at the bottom.
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then apply healing ointments to the healthy flesh until it is healed.
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit, et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	and if it is not healed by this method, then cauterize it as we have said; and if the bone is diseased from the fistula, cut it out.et s’il est a la jointure ou nerf ou artere, si le coupe et li ostes la fautreure, et si li os est corrompus, si le cope, et tu le ramettes s’il n’
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If a vein or nerve does not trouble your principal limbs, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee, puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	and if the bone is exposed and there is decay and blackness in it, then treat it with king's ointment until the decay is all removed, then heal it with healing things;
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant, saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	and if it does not heal and returns as before, know that you have not gone to the source:
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons, et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	if you uncover it and go to the bottom, and remove all the decay, then restore the place;
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	and if it is thus healed, that is good.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	If not, know that the decay is too deep for you to reach it;si le memre est trois ou quare disloquez, se il s’en peut aler, si covient que on le fasse aler et que il rent a
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	if the limb is dislocated three or four times, if it can be moved, then it should be moved and return to its natural position without any other artifice;
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles, si l’estrai a I estrument covenauble a ceu, et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	and if there is a small rotten bone, and you can pull it out with tweezers, then extract it with the instrument suitable for this purpose, and if there are many bones, pull them all out without leaving any behind.
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour, si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	and if moisture is causing the dislocation, and there is no error or fear, then cut and release the moisture and the flesh, and free the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture, et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os, et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	And if you cannot remove them in an hour, then put something on the wound that promotes pus, and let it fester around the bones, and then they will be more easily removed.
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse, si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee, puis restoure la plaie;	And if it is a large bone, such as in the leg or thigh, then clean only the corruption until all the blackness is removed, and then dress the wound.
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	And if there is a large part of it that is rotten, and it comes to the marrow of the bone:
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	if it needs to be bandaged and wrapped all the way up to the腐敗, and then treated until it is healed.
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint I home en sa jambe, si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	and I will tell you about a fistula that happened in a man's leg, so that you can take example and help in your work.
Il fut I jovencelz entor XXX ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors, tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	He was a young man of about 30 years old, who had pain in his leg due to a cause that came from inside the body, so that the matter came out through the leg, and it was swollen with a large abscess, and he did not know what to do to open it;
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri, et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	but the doctors worked so much on it that the abscess opened and a lot of matter came out, and it became a fistula, and many openings came from which all the pus and moisture of the body flowed out;
et maint mire i mirent cure entor II ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains, tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit, et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	and many doctors treated him for 2 years, and there was no improvement in his condition, so I was called to see his leg and the medicine with which he was being treated, and I saw that which flowed out through the openings caused great harm to the body;
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	and the bodies of the young men became red, and had a citron colour.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus, et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	I pitched a tent in one of these openings, and then searched all the openings, and found that one came against another all the way down the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os, et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	I hurried then, and probed one of the openings until I exposed a portion of the bone, and found it rotten and piercing through, with the corruption going right to the bone inside;
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	I probed what appeared to be of the rotten bone, and believed there was no other corruption except that which I removed;
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	and began to dress the wound with strong medicines for a long time, but it would not heal;
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant, et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	and then I began again, and exposed the bone as before, and found the corruption continued in the bone, and probed it, and then removed it, and laboured to heal the place;
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole, puis le restourai de medicines;	but I could not, for whenever I probed around a palm of the bone, and drew it out as far as its root, then I restored it with medicines;et je vis bien que ne demoureroit ains qu’il ne fist l’un de ces deux: ou il morroient par la corruption qu’il aveit en son corps, ou
et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment, et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir, et por la paour de mort que je avoie de lui.	and he was cured and healed quickly, and the procedure did not need to be repeated except for the weakness of the patient who could not endure it, and because of the fear of death that I had for him.
Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement, et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	For the bloodletting, he often bled profusely, but he was completely healed, and in the bone a hard lump grew, and he had a good disposition and no harm or contrary effect anywhere, neither lying nor moving.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if the bone is broken in any part of the body, then it should be treated in this way:
pren I liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert, et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	take a string and tie it to the head of the bone that is open, and have someone pull it upwards;
et met I autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os, et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz, et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	and tie another thicker string of linen to the first string, and tie it around the flesh above the bone, and pull on the head, so that you draw up the corrupted flesh from below, and uncover the flesh above where you want to operate, so that the string does not cut the flesh;
et met I tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	and place a hot coal or a small tablet under the bone to cover the corrupted flesh;
et covient tant soier com on puet veoir et sentir la corruption, et soier ancor autre fois.	and one must wait as long as one can see and feel the corruption, and wait again another time.
Et se li os est corrumpus, et n’apert mie, et li corruptions est en mileu ou en une partie, si descuevre la char toute;	And if the bone is rotten and does not open, and the corruption is in the middle or in a part, then cut away all the flesh;
puis met I tison desoz, et puis soie des l’une partie a l’autre la corruption, et soit li soieure dou lonc de la corruption I poc, si com nos avons dit;	then put embers underneath, and then feel from one part of the corruption to the other, and the sore will be drawn towards the embers, as we have said;
et se li corruptions est en la jointure, si cope la jointure corrumpue, et soie l’os ou elle contient de l’autre part;	and if the corruption is in the joint, cut away the rotten joint, and feel the bone where it contains from the other side;
et se li corruptions est en la continuation des II jointes, si n’i a autre angien que dou coper;	and if the corruption is along two joints, there is no other remedy but to cut them away;
et se li corruptions est ou poignil de la main, ou ou poignil dou piet, si est mout fort celle chose, mais toutevoie il covient que tu enquieres celle corrosion, coment elle t’apert;	and if the corruption is in the knuckle of the hand or foot, it is a serious matter, but nevertheless you must investigate the corrosion and how it appears to you;
et la mundifie en toutes les manieres que tu pues, mais que li voine ou li nerf ne te faicent contraire;	and cleanse it in every way you can, but be careful not to damage the vein or nerve.
et saiches que li incisoire et les soies por coper ces os sont maintes, selonc l’assise des os et l’aparance d’ous, et lor grossece et lor subtiliteit, et lor grandor et lor petitece, et lor duresce;	and know that the knives and saws for cutting bones are many, according to the position of the bones, their appearance, thickness, thinness, size, and hardness.
et por ceu covient il apareillier a chescune semblance d’ovraige son estrument;	and therefore one must prepare different tools for each type of operation.
et saiches que l’uevre te moustrera l’estrument dont tu avras mestier, selonc la conissance de cest art, et le tesmoignaige des manieres des maladies;	and know that the job will show you the tool you need according to your knowledge of this art and the testimony of the nature of the diseases;
si porpense l’estrument dont tu as mestier selonc ceu qu’il le covient.	if you think about the tool you need according to what is appropriate for it.
dou feu	fire
Li chiés porrissent ou par cause dedens, ou par cause defuer;	The shoulders may dislocate due to an internal or external cause;
et quant tu avras medicinee celle corrosion par la cure des medicines, et il ne profitent mie, si covient coper celui membre jusques au leu ou li corrosion vient, si que li malaides eschaipe par ceu de la mort, ou par la malice, qui est plus grans, de la defaute dou membre;	and when you have treated that corrosion with medicine, and it does not help, then you must cover that limb up to the place where the corrosion is, so that the patient escapes either death or the greater evil of losing the limb.
et li signes si est que li membres devient noir, si qu’il semble qu’il soit ars dou feu, et porrist aprés la noiror, pues va celle corrosions de membre em membre, et prent par tout le cors;	and the signs are that the limb becomes black as if it were burnt by fire, and then after the blackness, the rot spreads from limb to limb, and affects the whole body;
si te haste dou coper, et se c’est par la percussion d’aucunes venimouses bestes, si com scorpion de mer et wivre et semblans, se li corrosion est au chief dou doi, si le cope, et ne li doner mie espaice de venir jusc’a la main.	if it is from a bite, and if it is from the sting of some venomous creature, such as a sea scorpion, adder, or similar, if the rot is on the head, then cut off the hand, and do not give it any time to spread to the arm.
Et s’elle vient jusc’a la main, si la cope a la jointe, si que la corrosion ne viegne jusc’a bras;	And if it reaches the hand, then cut at the joint so that the rot does not spread to the arm;
et s’elle vient au bras, si le cope au coute;	and if it reaches the arm, then cut at the elbow;si elle viegne au coude, si la cope a la jointe de l’elbow
et s’elle passe le coute, c’est li mors, et n’i vaut amenistremens fuers que li quantitez de sa vertut;	and if it passes the elbow, that is death, and there is no remedy other than to cut off the quantity according to its strength;
et tot ensi fai quant li corrosion vient ou piet:	and do the same when the corrosion comes to the foot:
s’elle vient en la premiere jointe, si la cope aprés l’autre jointe;	if it comes in the first joint, then dislocate the cup after the other joint;
et s’elle vient ou piet, si cope tout le piet;	and if it comes to the foot, then dislocate all of the foot;
et s’elle monte en la jambe, si cope a la jointure dou genoil;	and if it rises in the leg, then dislocate at the knee joint;
et s’elle vient desus le genoil, si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier le malaide a mort;	and if it comes above the knee, there is no other remedy but to kill the patient with a blow;
et li maniere dou coper ou dou soier le membre si est que tu le lie desus et desoz, et estende uns menistres l’un des liiens aval, et uns autres ministres l’autre liien amont, et tu dessevre la char qui est entre les II liiens a I spatumile large, tant que li os soit descovers;	and the method of dislocating a limb is to tie it above and below, and extend one assistant's hand downward from the lower ligature, and another assistant's hand upward from the upper ligature, and you loosen the flesh between the two ligatures by a span, so that the bone is exposed;
puis le cope ou soie, et met de chescune part I drapeil de lin, si que li soie ne touche le leu sain, et viegne au malaide autre lesion et aposteme chaus.	then dislocate it and place a piece of linen on each side so that the bone does not touch the healthy spot, and cause another injury or abscess to the patient.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient quant tu oevres, si cauterize le leu hastanment, ou tu met sus aucunes poudres restraignans;	And if blood flow occurs when you operate, cauterize the site directly or apply some restraining powders.
puis revien a ta medicine tant qu’elle soit acomplie, puis lie le membre navreit d’un liien covenauble, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then return to your medicine until it is completed, then bind the wounded member with an appropriate ligature and treat it until it is healed.
et je te conterai k’il avint a I home en som piet:	And I will tell you what happened to a man in a dream:
il li avint une noiror qui sembloit arsure de feu, et celle corrosion vint premier en son doi dou piet, tant qu’elle porprist tout le piet;	He had a dark discoloration that looked like a burn, and this corrosion began at the bottom of his big toe, spreading to cover the entire foot;
et quant li hons vit la corrosion, si se hasta de coper le piet, et fut sanez;	And when the man saw the corrosion, he covered it with copper, and it was healed.
et lonc tens aprés li revint li corrosion ou doi de la main, et il vint a moi, et je li mis sus choses repercussives aprés la mundification dou cors, et ne pot cesser li corrosions;	Long after, the corrosion returned on his finger, and he came to me, and I applied some counter-irritant remedies after cleaning the body, but could not stop the corrosion;
et il vot que je li copasse la main, et je ne vou, que je avoie esperance de repercuter la matiere;	He wanted me to cover his hand, but I refused because I had no hope that the treatment would work.And he said: "If you do not want to treat it with counter-irritants, then cut off my hand." And I said to him: "If you were a king's son, I
et doutai ausi que se je tailloie sa main, qu’il ne morist, car li vertus de l’ome estoit foible;	and I doubted that if I cut off his hand, he would not die, for man's strength was weak.
et il se despera toz, et revint en sa terre, et se hasta de coper sa main, et fut sanez;	And they all despaired and returned to their land, and had their hand bound, and were healed.
et je n’ai ceu conteit fuers que por ceu c’on faice autreteil, s’on en a mestier.	and I have not found anything wrong with this except that one should not do it to someone else if they need it.
Aucune fois vient aposteme en leu charnut, et demore si longement qu’il fait grant assemblee de bowe;	Sometimes an abscess forms in a fleshy part, and remains so long that it causes a great gathering of pus;
et puis ront et perce, et en saut li bowe, et demoure li leus vuis, ausi com uns vasselz;	and then they rupture and discharge, and the place remains hollow like a vessel;
et li cuir qui est desus est ausi subtilz com I drapelz deliiez, et ne corront mie jusc’a l’os, ne jusc’au nerf, et telz maladie si est apelee «sain», et n’est mie apelee «fistule»;	and the skin above is as thin as a separated cloth, and does not reach the bone or nerve, and such a disease is called 'healthy', and not a 'fistula'.
mais s’elle est si alongie qu’elle viegne jusc’a l’os em parfont, si est apelee «fistule»;	but if it is so long that it reaches to the bone, it is called a "fistula".
et li cuire si est que tu cope celui cuir tout entor, et meismement quant il est subtilz, ausi com uns drapelz;	and the cautery should be applied all around the wound, especially when it is deep, just like a bandage.
et ne s’aert mie por sa corruption.	and do not worry about causing harm.
Et se tu as fiance que li cuirs s’aerde, et li corruption n’est mie en parfont, et li cuir est espés de char, si le cure de clistere ensi:	And if you are afraid that the skin will burn, and the corruption is not in depth, and the skin is thick, then cauterize it thus:
regarde se li seins est grans, et li bowe qui en ist est de puant odor, adonques le clisterize de medicine egiptiaine qui est ensi faite:	examine if the breast is swollen and the nipple has an offensive odor, then treat it with an Egyptian medicine made thus:
prenez aisil, et oile, et litargire, igalment, et metez cuire en I vassel au feu, tant que li medicine soit rouge, et deviegne ausi espesse com miel;	take asafoetida, oil, and litharge, in equal amounts, and put the mixture in a vessel over fire until the medicine turns red and as thick as honey;
et puis pren de ceu selonc ta necessiteit, et le font en aigue et en miel, et en clisterize lou sein, et estraint le pertus;	and then take some of this according to your need, and they make it in water and honey, and they administer it as an enema to the breast, and they constrict the opening;
et laisse la medicine ens par II houres, puis l’estrai en espreignant;	and let the medicine remain for two hours, then extract it by squeezing;
fai ce mout de fois, tant que li seins soit mondefiiez, et soit ostee li puor;	do this many times until the breasts are relieved and the poultice removed;
et aucune fois est clisterizeis d’aigue de cendres, quant ceste medicine n’est presens, et est que tu preignes cendres de fust de vigne, et giete aigue desus, puis la coule, et en clisterize, tant que tu saiches que li seins est bien mondez;	and sometimes they are enema with water of ashes when this medicine is not available, and it is that you burn vine wood to ashes, and pour water on it, then strain the liquid and use it as an enema until you know that the breasts are relieved;
et se li malaides ne le puet soffrir, ne la medicine egiptiaine ne l’aigue de cendres, si le clisterize d’aigue et de miel ou il ait un poc de litargire broiet;	and if the patient cannot bear it, or the Egyptian medicine, nor the water of ashes, then they are enema with water and honey in which there is some powdered quicklime;
ou tu la clistirize de miel et de vin melleit, que li mielz ait proprieteit de mundifiier et de laver, et li vins fait aerdre le sain;	or cleanse it with honey and wine, for honey has the property of cleansing and washing, and wine makes the wound breathe.
et quant tu as ce fait, et tu as fiance que li seins est bien mundifiiez, si le clisterize de ceu que fait naistre char en li, et est que tu preignes emplaustre diafinit, et le font avec oile roset et en vin;	and when you have done this and trust that the wound is clean, then cleanse it with that which makes bowels move within him, and it is what you prepare poultice of diafinit, and mix it with rose oil and wine.
ou tu le clisterize d’aucunes medicines et d’oignemens, dont j’ai dit les proprietez ou traitier des oignemens;	or cleanse it with some medicines and ointments, of which I have spoken of the properties in the section on ointments.
et se li pertus dou sein est petis, et li cainne dou clistere n’i puet entrer, si l’eslarge d’un fer un poc, et met ens une tente de l’oignement egiptiein, ou oignement basilicon, tant k’il soit eslargiez;	and if the wound of the breast is small and the pipe of the enema cannot enter it, then widen it a little with an iron, and put in it a tent made of egyptian ointment or basilicon ointment, as much as can be inserted.
et se li plaie est trop large, si la cout et i laisse tant soulement I leu ou li clistere puisse entrer, et se li pertus que giete bowe est au desus, si le cope ou plus bas leu que i est.	and if the wound is too large, then cut and leave only the place where the enema can enter, and if the orifice that vomits bowels is above, then cut it below, where it is.
Car quant li bowe est en parfont, si n’i laisse enjanrer char;	For when the bow is drawn fully, do not leave an arrow to lodge there.
et se tu ne pues coper lou sein desoz si com tu vues, si appareille en tel maniere que li bowe corre au plus bas leu que i est, car quant li bowe est parfont, si n’i laisse enjanrer char et se tu ne pues coper lou sein desoz si com tu vues, si apareille en teil maniere:	if you cannot cover the breast from below as you wish, then prepare in such a way that the bow points to the lowest place it can reach. For when the bow is drawn fully, do not leave an arrow to lodge there.
que li bowe corre legierement aval, et n’i lassier rien de la bowe;	let the bow move gently downward, and let nothing of the bow remain.
et pren medicines consolidatives por mettre sor le sain, et estent sus I drapeil de lin que cuevre tout le sain;	take consoliding remedies to apply over the wound, and they must be placed over the linen bandage that covers all the breast;
puis cope as forces endroit le pertus dou sein I poc plus large dou premier, pues estent oignement souef sus I autre drapel selonc la quantiteit dou pertus, et le met sus le pertus dou sain por aligier la bowe, et n’oster mie le grant drapeil fuers que aprés maint jor une fois;	then press firmly on the opening of the breast, making the hole as wide as the first one, then apply a suet ointment over the other bandage according to the size of the wound, and place it over the wound to ease the bow, without removing the large bandage for several days.
et celui qui est sor le pertus dou sein, oste sovent por oster la bowe, et saiches ceu que corra de la bowe, se c’est venin ou poc ou assez, ou digeste, ou indigeste;	and that which is on the nipple, remove often to take out the bow, and know what flows from the bow, whether it is venom or little or enough, or digestive, or undigested;
et pren warde se li patiens sent dolor ou nom, et s’il i a aposteme ou non, et quant ta medicine s’est en teil maniere estendue et tu vois la nature que saut sus le pertus dou sain, si saiches que li seins s’aert ja, et aproche li santez;	and take care if the patient feels pain or not, and if there is an abscess or not, and when your medicine has been applied in such a way and you see the nature that rises on the nipple, then you know that the milk is coming out, and approach the saints;
et puis le deslie le matin, ou le tier jor, et quant tu delies la plaie, si chainge I autre drapeil, et renovele l’oignement.	and then untie it in the morning, or at noon, and when you untie the wound, change the other bandage, and renew the ointment.
Et se li seins giete bowe indigeste aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie.	And if the breast milk flows in an unripe state after several days, know that the breast will not produce milk.
Et se venins subtilz cort aprés lonc tens, si ne te desperer mie de la santeit, car li santez aproche.	And if subtle poisons spread over a long time, you should not despair of health, for health is approaching.
Car il i a homes cui tarde enjanremens de char en ses plaies, et de ces que font le contraire;	For there are men whose wounds heal slowly with pus in their wounds, and those who heal quickly in the contrary way;
et se bowe indigeste saut dou sein aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie;	and if undigested milk flows from the breast after many days, know that the milk is not coming out;
et se li seins tarde d’aerdre, et est porloigniez, si ajoste medicines sechans moistes en substance et seches en vertut, si com oignement diafinit, car il i a grant partie de vitriole, et c’est li derriene medicine;	and if the breast is slow to heal and is distant, then apply dry medicines that are moist in substance but dry in virtue, like an ointment that is diaphanous, for it contains a large amount of vitriol, and this is the final medicine.
pren oignement dyafinit, et le font avec oile roset, et l’arose de viel vin igal en substance;	take diaphanous ointment, and make it with rose oil, and equal rose wine in substance;
puis le confit et en use;	then cook it and use it;
et ceu meisme fait mielz cuit engroissiez, quant oignemens dyafinit n’est presens, ou tu pren mirre et aloen et encens, et le broie, et le poudre sus le miel quant il est sor le feu;	and with the same make honey candy, when diaphanous ointment is not available, or take myrrh and aloe and incense, and grind them into powder over the honey while it is on the fire;
et puis en glue I drapel, et l’estent sor le sein, et aucune fois i aministre on aristologe longe, et racines de lis celeste, qui est ausi com farine de veces et centoire;	and then use this to glue a bandage onto the breast, and sometimes administer aristologus root, which is like flour made from vetches and centaury;
et en use de simples ou de compostes:	and use simple remedies or compounds:
broie les, et en fai poudre, et met sus le miel que j’ai dit, et en use;	grind them to powder, add the honey I mentioned earlier, and use it.
et se li cure est alongie, et n’est curez par ceste cure, adonc saiches que la corruptions est em parfont, et fait empression en l’os, ou as membres durs, ou as liemens;	And if the wound is deep and not healed by this treatment, then you will know that the corruption goes deep, causing impressions in the bones, or hard spots in the limbs or internal organs.
si le cure de la cure de fistule, si com nos avons dit ci devant.	if the wound is a fistula, as we have said earlier.
de l’aposteme de l’ungle	of the abscess of the nail
Panarice est un aposteme que naist desoz l’ungle dou pouchiet de la main, ou dou piet, ou par aventure naist en autres dois;	Paresis is an abscess that arises underneath the fingernail or toenail, or occasionally in other places. It can also arise in the armpit, or the groin, or the stomach, or between the buttocks, or on the back, or behind the ears, or anywhere else.
et quant il est envielliez, et on n’i prent garde, si i vient I aposteme chaus, et corront et giete bowe tant qu’elle corront la racine de l’ungle, et par aventure la corront toute;	And when it becomes infected and is left untreated, then an abscess forms, and it runs and oozes pus as long as the root of the nail is affected, and sometimes it affects the entire nail. This can also happen to a toe or any other finger. The same treatment should be applied to all such cases.
et vient li corrosions jusc’a l’os, tant qu’il i vient dolor puant, et est li chiés dou doi larges, et est li color fuxe.	and comes the corrosion to the bone, so that it causes a fetid pain, and the shoulder is made broad on both sides, and the color is yellow.
Quant tu le cures si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu copes a i. fer toute la superfluiteit qui est demoree de l’ungle, puis cauterize la plaie aprés.	When you treat it as we have described in the previous section, and the treatment does not help, then you should cut away all the excess tissue that is hanging from the nail, and then cauterize the wound afterwards.
Li cauteres est mout grans aide se li os est sains, et li ungle est sainne;	Cauteries are of great help if the bone is healthy, and the fingernail is healthy;
et se li ungle apresse la char ens, et l’encomence a poindre, et la blece, si covient que tu mettes lou rait desoz l’ungle que point la char, et la boute en haut, et cope celi char subtilment et legierement, et met sus le remenant de la char medicines ardans et corrosives por oster tout;	and if the nail pushes against the flesh and begins to grow out, and the blister, then you must put the thread under the nail pushing the flesh out, and pull it up, and gently and subtly cut off that flesh, and put on the rest of the flesh burning and corrosive medicines to remove everything;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then cure the wound until it is healed.
Et se li corrosion est en l’os, si le cope, et trai fuer, car tant com li os corrumpus i est, si ne puet saner;	And if the corrosion is in the bone, cut it out and draw it out, because as long as the corrupt bone remains, it will not heal;
et se tu vois le doi corrumpre, si le cope en I des nous si com il est devant dit, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and if you see the shoulder becoming corrupted, cut it out in the neck as previously described, then cure it until it is healed;
et s’il est ferus, et boutez, et il sent grant dolor, si covient que tu le sainnes premier;	and if it is wild, and bitten, and it feels great pain, then you must treat it first;
puis cope l’ungle dou spatumile agut en taillant de travers desus, et warde que li taille ne viegne jusc’a la char qui est desoz l’ungle, car li malaides sentiroit trop grant dolor;	then cut the nail of the thumb with an agaric, cutting diagonally across the top, and be careful that the cutter does not reach the flesh underneath the nail, for the patient would feel too much pain;
et s’il avient, si met chose sus qui apaise.	and if it happens, put something on it to soothe it.
la dolor dou sourdoit de la main	the pain of a deaf person's hand
Li dois ajostez qui naist en mains d’aucuns homes par aventure est toz charnus, et par aventure i a teil ou il a osses, et aucune fois i a ungle, et aucun d’aus naissent en la racine de la jointure, ou li naissance est en aucuns nous des dois.	The two joints that grow in some people's hands by chance are sometimes all flesh, and sometimes they have bones, and sometimes nails; and some grow from the root of the joint, and the growth is on some fingers.
Cil qui naist en aucune nout dou doi ne se muet, et cil qui naist a la jointure dou doi, par aventure se muet;	Nails which grow from the top of the finger do not move, but those that grow at the joint of the finger may move.
la taille de celui qui est charnus si est legiere, en teil maniere:	The cutting of one who is fleshy should be done thus:
taille le en sa racine d’un large spatumile.	Cut it at its root with a broad agaric.
Cil qui naist en la racine de la jointure si est grief a curer:	The one that grows at the root of the joint is difficult to treat:
si te tien dou coper.	if you hold it still.
En celui qui naist ou doit au derrien nout, si covient que tu copes premier la char reondement jusc’a l’os, puis cope l’os a une soie convenable a ceu, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	For those who are born in the back of the jaw, you should first scrape the round flesh to the bone, then scrape the bone with an appropriate needle, then heal it until it is healthy.
Li soudemens que vient as dois ensamble vient par naissance, ou par soudement de plaie, ou par arsure de feu, ou par semblans choses.	Joints can be united by birth, or by the joining of a wound, or by a burn, or by similar things.
Si couvient que tu copes celle soudeure, si que li doit repairent selonc lor formes naturelz;	You must cut this suture, so that the fingers grow according to their natural shape;
puis met entre dous tentes ou drapelz moilliez en oile roset, qu’il ne se soudent;	then place between two tents or moistened sheets in rose oil, so that they do not adhere.
ou tu met entre dous pieces de plonc subtilz, tant que li leus soit soudez, si com il covient.	or you put between two thin pieces of wood, until the glue dries, as it should be.
Se soudemens vient a aucun de ses dois avec la paume, si cope celle sodure si com il covient.	If adhesion occurs to one of his hands with the palm, correct that adhesion as it should be.
des vils	of the evil
Vis sont voinnes grosses envoloupees pleines de superfluitez melancoliouses, que vienent em plusors membres dou cors;	Veins are large, enveloped vessels filled with melancholy superfluities that come from various parts of the body;
et plus avient en jambes de ces qui vont a piet et qui travaillent et portent, que a autres.	and this happens more often in legs for those who walk and work and carry things, rather than others.
Il covient donques que tu li aministres aucune fois espurgement de cole, et puis le saine de la basilique.	Therefore, you should administer to him some purgative medicine, and then the basil drink.
Li cure de fer si est selonc II manieres:	There are two types of cautery:
l’une est c’on les cope, et traie on fuer le sanc noir;	one is done with fire, drawing out the black blood;
et li autre maniere si est que tu lieves la voinne, et la trai toute fuer.	and the other way is to lift the vein and draw it all out.
Li taille si est selonc ceste maniere:	The incision is done like this:
arose li premier la jambe d’aigue chaude mout fort, tant que li gros sans soit subtiliiez, puis estrain la jambe dou malaide des desus la cuixe jusc’a la partie desoz le genoil;	first, raise the leg with very hot water until the large veins are dilated, then straighen the leg from above the thigh to just below the knee;
puis cope la voinne en I leu, ou en II ou en III, d’une taille large, puis eslieve et trair fuer le sanc noir a ta main, des l’un chief jusc’a l’autre, tant que tant de sans en isse com li vertus dou malaide puet soffrir;	Then open the vein in place I, or II, or III, with a wide cut, then press and draw out the black blood into your hand, from one end to the other, until as much blood comes out as the illness can bear;
et puis la lie, et li comande qu’il se teigne de viandes enjanrant cole noire;	and then cleanse it, and instruct him to anoint himself with black pitch;
et recomence l’evacuation et la sainie quant les voinnes sont plainnes, et nuist au malaide.	and repeat the bloodletting and bleeding when the veins are full, which benefits the illness.
Li alevemens de li est selonc ceste maniere:	The treatments for this illness are as follows:
reis la jambe dou malaide, s’il i a mout de poil, puis le met ou bain, et li arose la jambe d’aigue chaude tant qu’elle deviegne rouge, et enflent les voinnes;	examine the leg of the patient, if there is much hair, then put it in the bath, and pour hot water on the leg until it turns red and opens the veins;
et se tu n’as point de baing, si le chaufe au feu, et puis le cope endroit la voinne dou lonc au chief dou genoil, ou en la partie desoz a la cheville;	and if you do not have a bath, heat it by the fire, and then open the vein from the long side of the knee to the top of the ankle, or in the part below the ankle;
puis aoevre le cuir a l’oncine, et escorche la voinne de chescune part, tant qu’ele apere quant on la sent;	then open the skin at the base of the fingernail, and scorch the vein on both sides until it appears when you feel for it.
et on la voit rouge et noire, et quant elle entre ou cuir si semble ausi com une corde blainche;	and you will see it red and black, and when it enters the skin it looks like a white cord;
puis boute le rait desoz, tant qu’ele soit alevee dou cuir, et puis la pent a l’oncine legier, puis le cope en I autre leu ensus III dois;	then tie off the vein underneath, so that it is raised up from the skin, and then cut it at the base, then clamp it in another place above in two places;
puis escorche le cuir sus la voinne tant qu’ele apere, puis la lieve au rais, si com tu as fait, et la pent a un autre uncine, si com tu as fait premiers;	then scorch the skin above the vein until it appears, then lift it up to the nail, just as you did before, and cut it at another nail, just as you did before;
puis cope une autre taille, ou plusors se tu en as mestier, puis la lieve, et la cope au doi dou piet, puis la trai et lieve jusc’a la seconde taille;	then make another cut, or several if you need to, then lift it up and cut it at the toe, then pull and lift up to the second cut;
puis l’estrai de taille en taille, tant qu’elle isse toute fuer, puis la cope;	then draw it out from cut to cut, until it comes all the way out, then tie it off;
et se tu ne la pues traire et lever, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil fort double, et la lie et la trai, et i boute desoz I rait, et torne ta main d’une part et d’autre, tant qu’il en isse;	and if you cannot milk and raise it, then put a needle on a very strong double thread, tie it and milk it, put it under the udder, and turn your hand from side to side until it comes out.
et garde qu’elle ne cope, car s’elle cope, si ne la puet on traire ne lever, et en vient nuisement au malaide;	and beware that she does not kick, for if she kicks, you cannot milk or raise her, and harm comes to the patient.
