Et quant ce avient a aucun, et tu vues savoir s’il sera sanez ou non, si pren warde se tu vois ses mains mollifiies et enflees et mortes, et ne les puet movoir ne estendre, et quant tu les poins d’une aguille, si ne lou sent.	And when this happens to someone, and you want to know if he will be healed or not, take note if you see his hands soft, swollen, and numb, and he cannot move or straighten them, and when you prick him with a needle, he does not feel it.
Saiches qu’il est mortelz em plusors dispositions, et s’il les muet et sent bien quant on les estraint et point, saiches que li jointure de l’os est sauve, et que li malaides iert curez, s’on i met cure.	Know that it is deadly in many cases, and if they are mute and feel nothing when you dislocate and prick them, know that the joint of the bone is saved, and that the illness is cured, if one applies a remedy.Si tu vois ses mains enflees et molles et que l’on les estraint et poigne, si sent bien et muent, saiches qu’il n’est pas guerez, car la mort y entre.
Et se semblans chose vient a l’espinee dou dos, et tu vues savoir s’il iert sanez ou non, si pren warde se li piez sont amollis, et se li accident i sont qui sont em mains, et sus lou dos saut ventositeit et egestion sens volonteit;	And if something similar happens in the spine of the back, and you want to know if he is healthy or not, take note if his feet are swollen, and if the symptoms are in his hands, and on his back there are wind and urination without intention;
et quant on l’a sovineit sus son ventre, si saut egestion sens volonteit.	and when he is lying on his stomach, there is urination without intention.
Et quant il est sovinez sus son dos et il vuet asseller, si ne puet.	And when he lies on his back and wants to sit up, he cannot.
Saiches qu’il est mortelz:	Know that it is deadly:
si ne laboreir mie en sa cure.	if you do not work on its cure.Quant li piez sunt amollis et le dos sanz egestion
Et se cist accident ne li vienent, si est li chose plus legiere.	And if this accident does not occur, then the condition is more minor.
Et li cure si est que tu rewardes s’il i a aposteme chaut, si met sus l’espinee oile roset ou oile de moieuf d’uef, tant qu’il soit apaisiez;	And if there is an abscess in the spine, then put rosemary oil or hen's egg yolk on it until it is soothed.
puis met sus un des emplaustres confortans et sechans, et le lie d’un liien, et comande au malaide a reposer;	then apply one of the comforting and drying plasters, and tie it with a cloth, and instruct the patient to rest.
et ne dorme mie sus celle partie ou il sent la dolor, tant k’il soit sanez.	and not to sleep on the part where he feels pain until he is healed.
Et se aucuns os se dessevre, si covient coper sus lou keur;	And if any bone dislocates, then it is necessary to cover the heart;
et oste l’os, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie, s’elle est grans, a une costure, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and remove the bone, then unite the two lips of the wound, if it is large, with a stitch, and the physician should apply ointment around the wound, until it is healed.
et se li chiés de l’os est brisiez, ki est apelez li «chiés de la kowe», se i boute ton pouchet de ta main senestre, et le met igal a l’autre main a ton pooir, puis met l’emplaustre et l’estele sus, se tu en a mestier;	and if the head of the bone is broken, which is called the 'head of the neck', if you force your left palm into a pouch shape, and place it equally in the other hand to your ability, then apply the plaster and bandage it up, if you need it;
puis l’estraint, et s’il i a os desevreit, si fent sus, et l’oste, et cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit sanee.	then they bind it up, and if there is bone exposed, they stitch it up, and the surgeon treats the wound until it heals.
de la brisure de l’os de la hainche	of the fracture of the bone of the hip
Poc avient que li os de la hainche soit brisiez, et s’il avient, si n’avient fuer c’un poc d’amenuisement au chief;	Sometimes the hip bone is broken, and if that happens, there will be some lessening in the thickness of the head.
et fent dou lonc, et decline au pardedens, et vient au malaide dolor au leu, et pointure, et enfle ceu que brise.	and they go to the bowels, and decline towards the armpits, and bring pain to the affected area, and numbness, and swelling in what is broken.
Et li restoration si est que tu estendes ta main sus, tant que tu soies sus la briseure;	And for the cure, you must extend your hand over the break;
et saiches quelz est li brisure et li figure de li;	and you must know where the break is and what its shape is;
et se li brisure est au chief soulement, si met igal cele brisure, tant qu’ele soit a figure natureil.	and if the break is only in the head, then put it back into place so that it is in its natural position and shape.Et s’il avient en la coillee, et li chief est dessoubre, si leve la coillee tant qu’ele soit sus la br
Et se li brisure est dou lonc, ou elle decline au dedens, si fai gesir le malaide sus son ventre, tant que li restauration de cele brisure te soit aparillie.	And if the fracture is long, or it tilts inwards, then have the patient lie on his stomach, so that the restoration of the fracture can be prepared.
Et quant tu l’avras mise igal, si met sus l’emplaustre, puis met sus une estele de fust ou de keur, et estraint la briseure, si qu’ele ne se mueve;	And when you have made it even, then put on the plaster, and then a splint of wood or horn, and hold the fracture steady so that it does not move.
et emple le leu desoz les costes, tant que li lieure soit igalz.	and apply it under the armpits as far as the elbow joint, until the arm is even.
Et comande au malaide k’il dorme sus son costeit sain, ou sus son dos.	And instruct the patient to sleep on his healthy side or his back.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si n’i tochier, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et met sus ceu que nos avons devant dit;	And if swollen abscesses appear, do not touch them until the swollen abscesses are reduced, and apply what we have said earlier.Et s’il y a paor ou dountance, si covient que li malsainz soit assesié en un leu clerguier, et qu’ele soit gardee par clergues, et que li clercs prie
et puis revien a la restauration, et l’estraint si com il covient, s’il n’i a nul mavais accident;	And then return to the restoration, and hold it as it should be, if there is no bad outcome;and li clercs preient li chiés d’un costé et d’autrè la man, tant que li membre soit igal.
et c’est li maniere.	And this is the manner of doing it.Et quant li malsainz est assesié
de la brisure de l’ajutoire	of the shoulder dislocation
Li adjutoires est ceu qui est entre lou coute et lou chief de l’espaule, et s’il est brisiez, si le doit on restorer selonc l’une des II manieres:	The shoulders are what is between the neck and the head of the shoulder, and if it is dislocated, it should be restored according to one of two methods:la premiere est que li malsainz soit assesié en un leu clerguier; et s’il y a paor ou dountance, si covient que li malsainz soit assesié en un leu clerguier, et qu’ele soit gardee par
dont l’une est que tu pren I fust plain de moiene groissor, selonc ceste forme:	one of which is to take a straight medium-sized stick, according to this shape:
Et lie as II chiés II liens, et les pent en haut, et siece li malaide sus I siege;	Tie his arms with cords, and hold them up, and seat the patient on the chair;
puis li giete som bras brisiet sus le fust, tant qu’il viegne a l’aissele, et ait em mi une corbeure de fust, puis pent sus aucune pesant chose ou li ministres l’estende aval;	then pour boiling water on his arms, as far down as possible, and place a cushion of wood under him, then stretch him out over something heavy so that he is stretched out downwards;
puis mette li mires la briseure igal a ses mains ensamble, tant que li briseure retorne si com il covient.	then the operator puts the broken arm back in place, making it even with his other hand, so that it is put back in its proper place.
Et li autre maniere si est que on sovine le malaide sus son hatereil, et li lie la main a son col, puis comande a .ij. ministres que li uns teigne ceu qui est sus la briseure a ses mains, et li autres teigne desoz a tout .i. liien, et estende chescuns a sa partie.	The other method is to have the patient lean forward onto his elbow, and tie his hand to his neck; then instruct two assistants, one to pull upward on what is above the break with both hands, and the other to pull downward at each end of the stick, pulling in opposite directions.
Et se tu vues que li estraction soit plus fors, si estraint I liien desoz la briseure, et sus la briseure, et estende chescuns des ministres a sa part.	And if you want the extraction to be more forceful, then press the ligament below the fracture, and above it, and stretch each of the muscles on their own.
Et se li briseure est prochiene au chief de l’espaule, si covient que tu mettes I liien moien desoz l’assele, et I autre vers lou coute, desoz la briseure;	And if the fracture is near the head of the shoulder, then you must put one cord under the armpit and the other towards the neck, under the fracture;
et ausi se li briseure est devers lou coute, si i covient mettre I liien legierement, sens labor, tant que li briseure soit igalz sus lou leu, et sus lou coute;	and likewise if the fracture is towards the neck, then you must tie it gently without exerting force, so that the broken arm is aligned with its position and with the neck;
puis met igal la brisure, si com il covient, et l’estraint, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	then put it back evenly, as it should be, and hold it there, if no abscess forms.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si ne l’estraindre mie jusc’a VII jors, et met sus lainne moillie en aisil et en oile roset, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez;	And if an abscess does form, do not hold it until the seventh day, and put soft lamb's wool in oil of roses on it, until the abscess is healed.
puis l’estraint, et li maniere de l’estraindre si est que tu mettes l’emplaustre sus la briseure, puis assemble le bras sus l’ajutoire, et met ta main sus l’espaule ou sus lou sein;	Then hold it, and the way to hold it is to put the ointment on the dislocation, then raise the arm above the shoulder, and put your hand on the shoulder or breast;
et met le drapeil, et estraint sus l’ajutoire, et sus lou bras, si que li bras soit en leu d’esteles, s’aucune chose ne le te deffent, ou se li os n’est muez.	and hold it tightly, and the cloth too, so that the arm stays in place, unless something moves it or the bone shifts.
Et se tu doutes que li os ne se mueve, si use d’esteles, et met sus la brisure une estele plus large et plus fort des autres, et ait entre chescune estele I doi d’espaice, et soit chescune estele si grans qu’elle passe la briseure III dois de chescune part;	And if you doubt that the bone has moved, use splints and put one splint wider and thicker than the others over the dislocation, with two fingers of space between each splint, and make sure each splint is as long as it needs to be to extend past the dislocation on both sides;
puis estrain sus les esteles, ensi com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre sus la briseure, plus fort et moins en aloignant.	then stretch them over the stars, as I said at the beginning of the chapter about fracture, more strongly and less by moving away.
Et se tu vois l’assise des esteles, et l’estrignement, si com nos avons dit, en l’oure que tu restoures le membre brisiet, et tu doutes l’aposteme chaut, si le laisse a liier jusc’a septime jor, si com nos avons dit;	And if you see the base of the stars and the stretching, as we have said, in the hour that you restore the broken member, and you doubt the hot abscess, then leave it to ligature until the seventh day, as we have said;
puis regarde chescuns III jors lou lien, que prurite ne enfleure n’i viegne au leu, ou li norrissemens ne puist venir au membre por ceu k’il est trop estrois.	then look at each of the three days at the bandage, that itching nor swelling comes to it, nor the growth can come to the member because it is too tight.
Si l’adrece, si com nos avons dit.	As the adage says, as we have said.
Et se nulz telz accidens n’i vient, si ne lou desliier fuer que aprés III jors ou plus, et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ait ses mains sus son stomac;	And if no such accident comes, then take off the bandage after three days or more, and let the patient sleep on his back, and have his hands on his stomach;
et met desoz l’ajutoire I cussin plain de laine igalment, et regarde chescune houre dou jor ou de la nut, que li figure dou membre brisiet ne se mueve, ou ne soit amollis li liiens;	and put under the shoulder a pillow of wool the same height, and look every hour of the day or night that the figure of the broken member does not move, or the bandage become slack;
si l’adrece par la vertu de medicine, et li done la viande que nos avons devant mis, en teil maniere que li viande soit au premier subtilz;	if he receives treatment through medical skill, and is given the food that we have mentioned earlier, in such a way that the food reaches the most subtle parts.
et quant il comance a reprendre, si soit grosse.	and when he begins to recover, then he can eat solids.
Et est costume que li ajutoire et li jambe doient estre repris en XL jors dou tout;	And it is customary that the shoulder and leg should be treated for 40 days altogether;
et adonques lou doit on desliier et aministrer bain et medicines d’oignemens por le leu adrecier.	and then one must loosen and administer baths and ointments to ease the joint.
Et se li estricture est laide et emboee, si demore a desliier L jors ou II mois.	And if the dislocation is severe and stuck, it will stay for 50 days or two months.
de la brisure du bras	Of the break in the arm
Li bras est compos de II os, qui sont apelez li dui «foscile», de coi li uns est petis, et est cil qui enseut le pouchet;	The arm consists of two bones, which are called the 'ulna', of which one is small and lies below the armpit;
et li autres est grans, et est cil qui est desoz, devers lou petit doi;	and the other is large, and is the one that lies above, towards the little finger;
par aventure brise li grans foscile soulement, ou li petis, et par aventure andui ensamble.	by chance it may be just the large ulna that is broken, or just the small one, or both of them together.
Quant li petis fosciles est brisiez, li restaurations est legiere, et li sanations;	When the small ulna is broken, the restoration and healing are easy;
et quant li grans est brisiez, si est li sanation male, et plus griés que quant il sont brisiez andui ensamble.	and when the bones are broken, then healing is difficult, and more painful than when they are only broken in one place.
Se c’est li petis foscile qui est brisiez soulement, si le covient poc estendre legierement, et mettre igal.	If it's only the small bone that's broken, one should gently extend and put it in place.Et s’il est brisié soulement li gros, li petis est a l’envers; il doit estre ramené a son leu.
Et se c’est li grans foscile, si le covient estraindre plus fort;	And if it is a tough bone, then it must be extracted with greater force;
et l’estende sus I cussin, et teigne le pouchet de la main plus haut des autres, et li petis dois plus bas des autres dois, et soit li malaides croisiez sus lui meisme, et I cussin devant lui plus haut, que li malaides ne soffre nule labor;	and he should be laid on a pillow, and the arm pouch higher than the rest, and the little finger lower than the other fingers, and the patient's crosswise body weight on him, and the pillow in front of him higher so that the patient does not suffer any strain;
puis estende li ministres som bras a la partie desoz a sa main, ou a I liien, et uns autres ministres a I autre au desus.	then the minister should extend his upper arm to the part under his hand, or to the elbow, and another minister to the other above.
Et puis le mette li mires igal, selonc sa millor forme.	And then put the minister equally, according to his best form.
Et se en la brisure a pieces, si met chescune en son leu, et s’il en i a nule desevree ke poigne lou keur, et tu ne la pues restorer en son leu, si fent sus et l’oste, si com nos avons dit devant.	And if there are pieces in the fracture, place each one back in its proper location; and if there is any dislocation, hold the heart, and reset the bone as we have described earlier.
Et se avec la briseure a plaie, je en ai parleit au chapistre singuler;	And if with the fracture there is a wound, I have spoken about it in a single chapter;
si pren la cure.	then take the cure.
Et se en l’encomencement dou restorement sorvient apostemes chaus, si glue I drapeil de cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire blainche, que ne soit mie ne trop durs ne trop molz;	And if in the beginning of recovery, pustules arise, then apply a dressing of cerate made from rose oil and white wax, not too hard or soft;
et lie I drapeil par sus subtilment, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez.	and I gently wrap it above, until the hot abscess is soothed.
Et puis oste lou cerote, et i met l’emplaustre de la poudre dou molin avec abun d’uef, pues met les esteles, et soit li estele de la briseure adés plus fors, et un poc plus large que les autres;	Then remove the poultice, and apply the plaster of flour with egg white, then place the bandages, and have the bandage for the fracture be stronger and slightly larger than the others.
et saiches que il doit avoir VI esteles ou bras em plusors dispositions:	And know that there must be six bandages on the arm in various places:
soit que li briseure soit en l’un des os, soit en II;	Whether the fracture is in one of the bones, or in two;
et estraint plus sus la briseure que autre part, et toz jors moins en aloignant, si com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre;	and holds more tightly over the fracture than elsewhere, and always less as it heals, as I have said at the beginning of this chapter;
et soient li drapelz que sont sus la briseure molz et moistes, et ne soient mie dur ne aspres;	and the bandages that are over the fracture must be soft and moist, and not hard or rough;
et soit li filz, dont il est estrains, de lin, ne trop gros ne trop menus, si com nos avons dit.	and the thread it is bound with, of linen, not too thick nor too thin, as we have said.
Et rewarde lou membre et lou liien aprés aucuns jors.	And re-examine the limb and the ligament after a few days.
Et se aucuns mavais accidens vient au membre, si com prurite ki vient au membre, si covient que tu aroses lou membre d’aigue chaude, tant que cil prurites soit apaisiez;	And if an accident occurs to the member, such as itching that comes to the member, then you should soak the member in hot water until the itching is relieved.
et laisse le membre ne mie estroit reposer.	and let the member not be bound but rest easy.
Et puis rencomence l’estrignement, et se li liiens est amolis et li os desevrez, et semblant chose, si l’adresce.	And then restart the stretching, and if the ligaments are softened and the bones loosened, and similar things, then address it.
Et se pren warde se li norrissemens ne puet venir au membre, por ceu qu’il est trop estrois, si covient que tu l’amollisses .i. poc, et laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant que li norrissemens i corre, et puis l’estraint.	And if you see that the nutrients cannot reach the limb because it is too tight, then you should loosen it a little and leave it like that for some days, until the nutrients flow, and then bind it again.
Et se nules de ces choses que nos avons dit ne vient au malaide, si ne lou desliier jusc’a XX jors.	And if none of these things that we have said come to the patient, then do not release him until 20 days.
ou enqui entor, puis li pent les mains a son col, et soit ses cols igalz, et se warde de movement et de degitement, et dorme sus son dos;	or in this position, he can place his hands on his neck, and let his necks be even, and guard against movement and dislocation, and sleep on his back;
et saiches que ceste briseure est restoree en XXX jors ou en XXXV, et par aventure en XX jors, selonc les compositions et les complexions des vertus.	and know that this broken bone will be healed in 30 days or 35, and perhaps in 20 days, according to the combinations and complexes of the virtues.
de la brisure de la main	of the fracture of the hand
Saiches que au dos de la main et as nous des dois avient poc de briseures, et n’i vient mais que ploieure maintes fois.	Know that in the back of the hand and at the base of the fingers there are few fractures, and they only come from manyfold folds.
Et quant li plante de la main est brisie ou ploie, si covient que li malaides siece croisiet, et siet droitement devant lui igalement;	And when the palm of the hand is broken or bent, then the patient should place his arms in a cross position and stand upright in front of him, evenly.
puis met sa main sus la toie estendue, et estende li ministres les os brisiez, et les mete igalz li mires, tant qu’il soient bien joint;	Then he should put his hand on the ground stretched out, and stretch the minister's broken bones, and make them even with each other, so that they are well joined;
et met l’emplastre et les estoupes, se apostemes n’i vient, puis i met une estele selonc la quantiteit dou leu;	and put on the plaster and the bandages, if no abscesses develop there, then he puts on a splint according to the amount of space available.
et soit envoloupee en I drapeil de lin.	and is wrapped in a linen cloth.
Et se li briseure est au pardedens entor lou ventre de la plante, si fai une spere de drapelz, et comande au malaide qu’il l’estrigne a sa plante brisie;	And if the fracture is on the side of the body around the belly, make a sphere out of bandages, and instruct the patient to press it against their fractured side.
et puis l’estrain d’un lonc drapeil, et soit li estele de keur souef ausi grans com li plante de la main, et l’estraint, si com il covient.	Then he pulls on a long bandage and the splint should be made of soft wood as large as the palm of the hand, and he presses it against the fracture, just as it should be.
Et se li brisure est au defuer, si covient que tu mettes une estele sus, et une autre desoz en la plante, si que li mains soit overte et droite, puis le lie tot entor la main, et estanche lou liien entre les dois.	And if the fracture is in the forearm, then you should put a splint on top and another underneath the plant, so that the hand is open and straight; then tie it all around the hand, and stop the bleeding between the two.
Et se li briseure vient a aucun des nous des dois, se c’est li pouchés, si le met igal, si com il covient;	And if the fracture is in one of the fingers, then he puts it straight, just as it should be;
et l’estraint avec la plante, et se tu vues si met une estele droite petite por lever la briseure, et ne se mueve;	and he presses against the side, and if you see that a small straight splint is placed to lift the fracture, and it does not move;
et se li brisure est as autres dois, si com en l’indice ou l’un des autres, si le met igal, et lou lie avec lou doi sain qui est aprés;	and if the fracture is in another finger, such as the index or one of the others, he should make it even and bind it with the healthy finger next to it;
ou tu les lie toz en I tenant, que mues vaut, ou tu met sus une estele, si com ou pouchet;	or you can tie them all together in a bunch, or put a splint on it, such as a little bag;
et pren warde en la restauration et en la disposition d’aposteme chaut, et secor ceu qui i vient, si com j’ai dit.	and take care in the restoration and in the preparation of a hot abscess, and treat those that arise, as I have said.
de la cuixe brisie	of the broken thigh
Li os de la cuixe est maintes fois brisiez, et bien le voit on quant elle torne devant et derrier;	The thighbone is often broken, and one can see it when it turns forward and backward;
et li restauration si est c’on lie I liien desus la briseure, et I autre desoz.	and the restoration is that one binds the broken bone above, and the other below.
Et li malaides gise sus sa faice, puis estende chescuns ministres son lien a sa part igalment;	And let the patient lie on his face, then extend each band evenly on its own part;
et c’est quant li brisure est emmi l’os.	and that is when the fracture is within the bone.
Et se li brisure est prochiene a la racine de la cuixe, si soit li uns des liiens devers lou poignil, et li autres liiens desoz la briseure.	And if the fracture is close to the hip joint, then one ligament should be directed towards the buttock, and the other ligament beneath the fracture.Et li auter liiens que est sous le cotil, qu’il soit vers la cuixe.
Et ausi s’elle est prochiene au genoil, et adonques soit li liens delez lou genoil, et soit li extension aval;	And if it is near the knee, then let the band be above the knee, and the extension below;
puis mette li mires l’os igal a ses II mains, tant qu’il soit selonc sa figure natureil, et puis met l’emplaustre, et lou lie, se apostemes chaz n’i vient.	then put the mirror to the bone equal to his two hands, so that it is according to its natural shape, and then apply the ointment, and bind it, if no abscess comes out.
Et s’il i a aposteme chaut, si le laisse apaisier puis revien a ton ovraige et a ta cure;	And if there is a hot abscess, let it calm down, then return to your work and treatment;
li lieure est faite en teil maniere.	the ligature is made in such a way.
Il covient que tu envoloupes sus la briseure I bendeil dur doublé en II ou III, et en demoure li superfluitez, puis torne la jambe tant que li talons veigne a la racine de la naige, et boute I fil lonc entre la cuixe et la jambe, delez lou genoil desoz, et veignent li chief dou fil au desus;	You must wrap the break with a tough double folded bandage in 2 or 3 places, and leave off the excess, then turn the leg so that the heels come to the root of the toe, and insert the long thread between the thigh and leg, below the knee, and let the end of the thread come above;
puis torne sus la jambe et sus la cuixe le bendeil, puis met sus la briseure esteles, et met une estele sus l’os de la jambe;	then turn the bandage around the leg and thigh, then put splints on the break, and put a splint on the bone of the leg;
puis emple le leu vuit entre la jambe et la cuixe de drapelz souef por mettre igal l’estrignement, puis comence a liier forment III tors ou IIII sus la briseure;	then take eight inches of soft fabric between the leg and thigh to even out the strain, then start binding tightly three times or four times above the break.
et quant plus vas en sus de la briseure, et moins l’estraint;	and as you go higher above the break, lessen the strain;
puis enten as II chiés dou fil que tu as bouteit entre la jambe et la cuixe, et en lie III esteles que sont desus, puis revai au desoz au chief dou fil, tant que tu veignes delez le piet;	then tie two ends of the thread that you have taken between the leg and thigh, then tie three knots that are above, then go back down to the bottom of the thread, as far as the foot;
et l’estraint, si qu’il ne se mueve de son leu, puis le laisse ensi, puis k’il n’i vient ne aposteme ne enfleure n’autre semblant.	and tighten it so that it does not move out of place, then leave it as it is, so that no abscess or swelling or other similar thing comes.
Et s’il i avient, si le deslie, et adresce ceu que i vient, si com nos avons dit maintes fois;	And if something happens to it, then untie it and fix what is wrong, as we have said many times;
et se il i a pieces de l’os que poigne, si le covient ewer, s’om puet;	and if there are pieces of bone that poke out, they should be removed, if possible.
et s’on ne puet, si covient fendre le leu, et traire fuer;	and if one cannot, then one must split the area and pull it out;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant k’il soit sanez.	and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Et aucune fois est brisie li cuixe ensi c’on i met esteles, si com en l’ajutoire et ou bras;	And sometimes the thigh is broken in such a way that one puts in nails, like in the shoulder and arm;
toutevoie, en la restauration ensi faite ne cloche mie li malaides.	Nevertheless, this restoration does not cure the disease.Et s’il est de si grant force ke il ne se puet demourer a leu, si convient adés le
Et saiches que li cuixe est restoree en .l. jors, ou poc moins ou poc plus, selonc les diversitez des complexions.	And you shall know that the hip is restored in one day or a little less or a little more, according to the diversity of complexions.
de la ruelle dou genoil	of the groove of the knee
Saiches que en la ruelle dou genoil avient poc brisure, mais elle ploie maintes fois.	Know that in the joint of the knee there is little breaking, but it bends many times.
Et s’elle brise, si n’est mais c’une fendure, ou I pertus, et avient a tout plaie, et sens plaie, et ce sent om bien.	And if it breaks, it is only a split, or a perforation, and it happens to all wounds, and without wound, and this feels good to everyone.
Et li restauration si est c’on mette igal ceu qui est rons a ses dois, tant qu’il soit assemblez mues c’on puet;	And the restoration is such that one puts an equal weight on his fingers, as long as he can bear it;and if he cannot bear it, then he must dislocate it again.Et s’il est en la main ou au pie, et qu’il soit de si grant force ke il ne se puet adés remuer, si convient il que tu le
puis met l’emplaustre, et i met une estele reonde, se tu en as mestier, et l’estraint si com il covient, puis rewarde toutes les dispositions que nos avons dit ens autres briseures, si com aposteme chaut et autre semblant;	And if it is in the hand or foot, and it is of such great force that he cannot move it at all, then you must first put the plaster on, and a round nail if necessary, and bind it as it should be, then follow all the instructions we have given for other fractures, like hot abscess and similar.Et s’il est en la main ou au pie, et qu’il soit de si grant force ke il ne se puet adés remuer, si convient il que tu le puis met l’emplaustre, et i met une estele reonde, se tu en as mestier, et
si met a chescun accident ceu k’il li covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then put on each dressing as it is needed, until he is healed.
de la brisure de la jambe	of the fracture of the leg
Saiches que en la jambe ait II os, de coi li uns est apelez par droit non «mustelz», et li autres est apelez «foscile»;	Know that in the leg there are two bones, one of which is properly called the "muster", and the other the "foscle".
et avient tout auteil briseure com il vient au bras, et por ceu est li restauracion si com celle dou bras igalment, et li ovraiges est tout i. Et se li dui os sont brisiet ensamble, si torne li jambe de toutes pars.	and all the other injuries are as they are in the arm, and their restoration is also the same, and the operations are the same too. And if both bones are broken together, then the leg is twisted all over.
Et se li os subtilz est brisiez, si torne devant.	And if only the small bones are fractured, then it turns forward.
Et se li gros os est brisiez, si sent on grant dolor, et le voit on bien;	And if the large bone is broken, great pain is felt, and it can be seen clearly;
et torne desoz.	and it turns inside out.
Adonques amenistre extension, et le met igal, et lie les esteles igalement;	Therefore apply traction, and put it back in place, and bind the splints evenly;
mais toutevoie, il covient se li brisure est laide, et il i a plusors pieces, que li extension soit menor et plus legiere;	However, if the fracture is bad, and there are several pieces, then the traction should be lighter and gentler;
et l’alige selonc ta vertu.	and heal according to your power.
Et quant tu as tout acomplit ton ovraige, si pren II faixes de fust chevees que porpreignent la jambe d’une part et d’autre, et soient dou lonc de la jambe des le genoil jusque desoz;	And when you have finished your work, take two bundles of wood shavings that are purple-dyed at one end and white at the other, and let them be as long as the leg from just above the knee to just below.
puis envoloupe en II leus I bendeil desus et desoz, et le lie em mileu ausi, et a ceste lieure ne pora li jambe decliner a destre ne a senestre, et ensi est bien;	Then wrap two bands of linen around them, one above and one below, and also at the middle, and at this point he will not be able to bend his leg to the right or left, and thus it is well.
et aucun i aministrent I bers dou lonc de la jambe, et s’est de fust, et i met on la jambe por warder de movement, et proprement fait on ceu en la brisure ou il a plaie;	and some apply an oil made from fir wood, and they put the leg in a splint to prevent movement, and they properly apply this to the break where there is injury;
et remue chescun jor la jambe, por veoir s’il i a aposteme chaut n’autre accident;	and every day move the leg to see if there is any hot abscess or other accident;
si le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	until it is healed.
de la brisure des os dou piet	from the fracture of the bones of the foot
A la cheville ne vient point de brisure, mais as os dou piet vient aucune fois brisure et as dois poc, et n’i avient fuer que quassure em plusor dispositions.	At the ankle there is no fracture, but at the metatarsal bones there can sometimes be a fracture, and it occurs in various ways.
Et s’il avient as os dou piet brisure, et tu vois ces os sormonter l’un l’autre, si mette si malaides som piet sus la terre, ausi com s’il voloit aler, et puis met maintenant ton piet sus lou sien, lai ou li os sont levez, puis le presse tant k’il reveignent en lor leus;	If it happens that the bones of the foot are broken, and you see one bone on top of another, then place your foot upon the ground as if you wanted to walk, and then put your foot on his, where the bones are raised, then press until they return to their places.
puis met l’emplaustre et estoupes sus, et met desoz lou ventre dou piet une petite tauble a II chiés plains, puis l’estraint au piet avenanment, puis que tu as envoloupez drapelz entor, et autres choses dont tu as mestier.	Then apply the ointment and bandages on top, and place a small flat stone beneath the sole of the foot, then tighten it in a cast, and after you have wrapped cloth around it, and any other things you require.
Et quant .iij. jors ou .iiij. seront passez, si deslie lou liien, car tu troveras les os igalz, soient brisiez, soient desaluez.	And after three or four days have passed, loosen the binding, for you will find the bones healed, whether broken or dislocated.
Et s’il i a aucuns des dois brisiez, si les restoure, si com nos avons dit as dois de la main;	And if there are broken fingers, restore them as we said for the fingers of the hand:
puis met au doi brisiet une estele selonc la longesce dou doi, et soit un poc plus large, puis met desoz le piet celle tauble que j’ai dit, et l’estrain avenanment;	Then place a splint along the length of the broken finger, and let it be a bit larger, then place that flat stone beneath the foot as I described, and tighten it in a cast.
et s’il en i a II ou III, ou plus, brisiez, si met sus chescun doi une estele selonc sa quantiteit, envoloupee en I drapeil de lin, et estraint la tauble desoz lou piet;	and if there are 2 or 3, or more, broken, then put on each toe a plaster according to its quantity, wrapped in a linen cloth, and hold the table under the foot;
et soit estans sus lou chief de la tauble defuer lou ventre dou piet, si qu’il le teigne bien.	and be standing on the top of the table from under the belly of the foot, so that it holds it well.
Et covient que tu n’oblier mie les autres choses que j’ai dit as autres briseures, des que nos avons dit;	And you must not forget the other things that I have said about other fractures, which we have discussed;
et secor chescun accident si com il covient.	and treat each condition as it should be.
de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	of the break in the bone of the elbow
Quant li os de la nature la femme est brisiez, si la fai seoir enlargie, puis l’encline a la partie dou dos, et soit tenue par derrier;	When the bones of a woman's pelvis are fractured, have her sit with her legs apart, then lean forward from the waist, and be held from behind;
puis emplisse li baile la nature de la malaide de couton, et en i mette ausi gros com I sto;	then fill the pelvic area with cotton, and put in it as much as a stone;
puis deboute la femme, et lieve lou dos poc et poc, et adonques saut li coton, tant qu’il vient a l’entree de la nature, et revient li os avec lou sto;	then stand the woman up, and loosen the back little by little, and then jump the cotton, until it comes to the opening of the pelvis, and the bones return with the stone;
et quant elle vuet pissier, si oste lou coton, et quant elle a pissiet, se li remette, et ensi faice VII jors ou entor:	and when she wants to urinate, remove the cotton, and when she has finished urinating, put it back again, and do this for seven days or so:
si sera restoree li brisure, et se tu vues, pren une vessie de berbis, et lie au pertus une cainne, et boute toute la vessie en la nature;	the fracture will be restored, and if you wish, take a lamb's bladder, and tie it at the opening with a string, and fill the whole bladder with natural urine;
puis soffle en la cainne forment, tant que li vessie soit enflee dedens:	then blow into the pipe firmly, until the bladder is swollen inside:
la nature si revenra li brisure;	the natural state will return to the fracture;
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then fill it with cotton and leave it like that for a few days, until it is healed.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	And when the bone of the finger of a man or woman is broken, restore it in the same way as we have said for the bone of the hip;
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	and they are not hidden from those who devote themselves to it and understand my book.
Car li brisure li signifie em plusors dispositions la droite voie de la restauration:	For the fractures indicate, with many dispositions, the right way to restoration:
enten le donques.	 understand it therefore.
En la verge, quant elle est brisie, pren une gorge d’oie et i boute la verge;	In a penis that is fractured, take a goose's gullet and insert the penis into it;
puis envoloupe drapelz entor, et le laisse III jors ou enqui entor, et il sera sanez hastanment.	then wrap cloth around it, and leave it for three days or more, and it will be healed quickly.
de brisure avec plaie	from a break with wound
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	It is necessary for one who has a break with a wound, especially if it is large, such as the thigh or shoulder bone or similar, that they be bled immediately, in accordance with the bleeding we have described earlier.
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the wound bleeds, then resume reducing the dislocation in that same hour or that day, if no abscesses form.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	And if abscesses form, then leave it until the third or fourth day, as long as the abscesses are relieved; do not touch it on the second day, nor the third, for you would bring about a bad accident.
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	And if the broken bone is visible on the uncovered chest, you should gently touch it with your hands, making small movements.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	And if you cannot move it into place with your hands, then reset it using an instrument of iron which is seven or eight inches long, and the width depends on the size of the wound;
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	and for this reason it is necessary to use an instrument that is three or four inches wide, according to the need in each case of a fracture;
et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	and let it be rounded and a little thick so that it does not bend when you press it against the limb during your work, and let it be pointed at the end, and thicker at the middle towards the front, thus;
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	And it is called "palainche", because the curved head of the bone should be placed on the visible part of the skull;
et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	and then press down until it returns, and make them even against each other.
Et se li brisure est subtilz, et li estrumens ne puet bien prendre l’os, si covient que tu copes lou chief de l’os, tant que li estrumens en ait possance.	And if the break is subtle, and the instrument cannot well grasp the bone, then you must shave the head of the bone, so that the instrument can get a grip.Et se li chiés sont desaloiez a cause de moistor, et on les remettra et il n’i demourra pas, mais revient adés et desalue par petit mouvement qui advient, si convien que tu disloques la première fois.
Et se tu ne pues ramener l’os, si com nos avons dit, si lou cope d’un estrument covenable a ceu, ou incisoire ou soieure, a ton pooir;	And if you cannot reset the bone, as we have said, then use the end of a suitable instrument, whether an incision knife or needle, to your ability;
puis reis ceu qui est demorez en l’os d’aspreteit et de menues escorces.	then scrape away what remains in the bone of asperity and small fragments.
Et quant li os est ramenez, et li malaides sent grant dolor aprés, saiches qu’il n’est mie en son leu natureil.	And when the bone is reset and the patient feels great pain afterwards, know that it is not in its natural place.
Si fai tant qu’il soit en son leu, puis moille I drapeil en vin stiptique noir, et proprement se c’est en esteit;	Do this until it is in its place, then soak the cloth in red wine vinegar, and apply it clean if it is soiled;
et ne mettre mie sus la plaie cerote ne autre chose ou il ait oile, qu’il n’i faice venir porriture et corruption;	and do not put any ointment or other thing on the wound except oil, lest pus and corruption come from it;
puis aministre esteles quant tu as restoreit l’os, et laisse la plaie descoverte, et cope la coverture tout entor, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et te done bien en garde que li plaie ne soit estrainte avec la brisure;	then bandage the patient once you have reset the bone, and leave the wound uncovered, and wrap the cloth around it according to the size of the wound, and take great care that the wound is not pressed upon with the bandage;Et si tu vuoilles mettre cerote ou oile sus la plaie, ou il t’appartient, qu’il n’i fust porriture ne corruption.
et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	and many times this has been done by fools, and sometimes brought about the death of the patient or corrosion;
et soit li estrignemens plus molz et plus souef des autres brisures.	and it is the most painful and most severe of all fractures.
Et se li plaie est male ou grans, et tu doutes que mavais accidens n’i veigne, si com nos avons dit, et tu trueves dolor au leu, si n’i covient mie mettre sus esteles;	And if the wound is large and you doubt that an accident might occur as we have said, and you find pain in the area, then you should not put anything on it;
mais envoloupe entor, en leu d’esteles, drapelz durs, et les lie.	but wrap around, instead of stabs, hard cloth, and tie them.
Et quant tu vois aprés I jor ou II enjanrer bowe a la plaie, si oste ceu que tu as mis sus a tout vin, et i met oignement sanant plaies, si com oignement tetrafarmaçon et semblans.	And when you see after one or two days pus forming on the wound, then remove what you have placed over it completely, and apply an ointment that heals wounds, such as tetra-pharmacon and similar remedies.
Et covient que tu deslies lou membre .ij. fois le jor, lou matin et au vespre, tant qu’il soit soudez et sanez.	And it is necessary to loosen the limb twice a day, in the morning and at evening, until it is healed and closed.
Et covient que li membres soit aparilliez en teil maniere que li bowe corre aval legierement.	And it is necessary that the limb be prepared in such a way that the bowstring runs smoothly and lightly.
Et se maint jor trespassent, et il ne puet souder mais rent adés bowe, saiches k’il i a petites pieces d’os, por coi il covient que tu quieres la plaie avec tente, et oste toutes ces pieces desevrees que font venir celle dolor.	And if they go astray for many days, and it cannot heal but keeps going back and forth, know that there are small pieces of bone, because of which you should probe the wound with a tent and remove all these dislocated pieces that cause the pain.
Et se fistule vient au leu, ou autre maniere de corruption, si covient que tu le cures, selonc ceu qu’il dist en son chapistre ci devant.	And if a fistula or any other kind of corruption occurs, you should treat it according to what he said in the chapter above.
Et quant li os est brisiez, et apert sus lou membre, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire, et autres semblans des grans membres, si ne le traire mie, car maintes fois en vient li mors, mais le laisse tant qu’il porrisse;	And when the bone is broken and open on the limb, as in the thigh or shoulder, and similar large limbs, do not draw it out, because many die from that, but let it be until it heals;
par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	perhaps it will fall out after 20 or 30 days, then cure the wound if you can;s’il reste ades, tant qu’il ne porrisse, mais le lie entor, et en li leu qu’il
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	and if you cannot, then leave it.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	of bruises that come on the healing site
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	There often comes after the healing of the fracture, especially when it is near the joint, and it is an ugly sight to see the limb deformed;
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	and sometimes the limb cannot perform its natural functions.
Pren warde donques se li nous est fres:	So take care then when we are young:
si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	if the doctor prescribes astringent medicines like aloes, incense, myrrh, sarcocolla, and similar things, so that you mix some of these things together, or all together, and infuse them with styptic wine, or egg white, or garlic;
et les met sus le nout en estoupes, et l’estraint bien, et ne la desliier en mains jors;	and apply them to the navel as a poultice, binding it on tightly and not removing it for several days;
et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	then remove it and start again with another one, until the swelling is gone;
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	or you can use a well-made splint;
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	for the properties of the splint are such that it removes all swelling from the limbs;
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	and if the knotting has turned into hardness like stone, and it needs to be removed, then cut away at it, and the excess will become apparent;
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	or you can have a barber shave it so that it is removed, and treat the area until it is healed.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	of the limb which is weak after healing
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	When the fracture of the bone is restored, and remains after the limbs become weak and sottish, this happens for many reasons:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	one reason is that it was bound too tightly, and not as it should have been;
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	or because there were too many ligatures, and the limb could not receive nourishment;
ou por multitude d’arosement;	or from excessive moisture;
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	or from too much movement, not in its proper time;
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	or because he has little blood in his body and is weak.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	And the treatment is that you should have the patient eat, and make his body warm, so that his blood is multiplied within him;
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	and give him a bath, and joy and leisure;
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	then apply pitch to the limb so that it attracts a great deal of warmth, and often bathe it in warm water, until the warmth penetrates the limb;
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	and it returns to its natural shape.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	the limb bent after health
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	When the limb is twisted after being reset, and the broken bones are still open, and the shape of the limb is ugly, nevertheless it does not lose its natural function:
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	if you do not believe the fools who say that one must break the limb again from the start, and many fools have indeed done this in our land;
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	and this work is blamed, and great harm comes from it, and sometimes death;
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	Nevertheless, if the dislocations and wounds are fresh, then they should be washed with hot water or herbs that soften, such as leaves of marsh-mallow, roots, and honeysuckle, and similar things;
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	and make a soothing ointment, such as well-prepared diaquilon, and take the mucilage of marsh-mallow, and confit it with goose fat or olive oil, and apply it to the wound;
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	Or take fat figs, and crush them with colon dung, and similar remedies that soften quickly.
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	And sometimes the dislocation is caused by continually and constantly rubbing with moist hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	And every hour, movement must be applied to the limb.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	And if the wounds are old and hardened like stone, and need to be cut with iron, then they should be covered all the way to the bone, with a subtle incision lightly;Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	and put trust and study into the cure.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	Here begins the book of dislocations.
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocation occurs when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing the patient great pain and injury.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation comes to someone, one must immediately reset it without delay.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	For if one delays, the place will swell, and perhaps one will put it back out of place.
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	Therefore, one must not move it when it is swollen:
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	many times causing spasms and other pains;
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	Nevertheless, when this happens, let the patient bleed, then leave him, until the abscesses are opened;
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	then warm the limb with hot water and oil, then reset it gently, and treat each joint as the cure will come into its place.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	And I have arranged the chapters on dislocations from the head to the feet.
des mandibules	of the jaw
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	Sometimes the jaws are dislocated downwards, and the dislocation of both is according to two manners:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	either they are slightly pushed out of their sockets, and softened a little;
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	or they are fully dislocated, hanging down towards the bottom, and drooling saliva from his mouth which he cannot hold in, nor close his mouth, nor control his tongue with speech.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When the dislocation is minor, it can be treated with various remedies.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	And if it is entire and complete, then you must reset it quickly, and not tarry at all;
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	and in such a way that the assistant grasps the head of the patient, and thrusts his fingers of one hand into the root of the jaw at the dislocation within the mouth, if the dislocation is on both sides;
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	and the other two hands should be used to apply pressure equally;
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	and instruct the patient to relax his jaws and move them in all directions.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	And he applies the cautery evenly until it returns to its place.
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	And if the reset is painful, especially if both jaws are displaced together, then they should be soothed with hot water and oil until they can be reset gently;Et s’il ne puet endurer la douleur de li ramener, et qu’il soit a grevance de sa vie, si le mets on une corde a l’entorn de li col et tire li cordons tant qu’il se ramene a son chief et qu’
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	And if he cannot endure the pain of the reset, and it threatens his life, then put a rope around his neck and pull the ropes until his head is
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	And when they are brought back evenly, and the mouth of the disease is closed well without softening, then place on wet cloths a poultice made of rose oil and wax, then bind it lightly with soft bandages.
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	and let the patient sleep on his back, and let his shoulders be between two pillows so that he does not move them to the right or left, nor try to move his arms, but eat soft food until the pain is gone and the jaws are numbed.
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	and then he can eat whatever he wants softly, and not to struggle to open his mouth to eat and drink until the mandibles are well numbed and healed.
Et se les .ij. mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	And if the two mandibles cannot be reset within an hour and are not converted to their place, then fevers and usual sores come, and possibly stomach problems, and possibly vomiting clear fluid.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	And when you see this, then you will know that it is pernicious;
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	and often the person dies within nine days.
de la forcelle	of the fork
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The foreskin cannot be cured by cauterization near the glans or foreskin, and sometimes it is cured by cauterization further away, and one feels it well.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	And the restoration is such that the patient lies on his back, and extends his arms;
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	and then press the area firmly with your palm, and it will return;
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	then apply the plaster and bandage, and bind it tightly;
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	and the shoulder which is towards the neck cannot dislocate;
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	if not, and if it dislocates even once, then reset it to its place as we have said;
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	then apply the plaster and bandage, and bind it tightly, and instruct the patient to rest until he is healed;
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	and in the same way, the shoulder of the spine is reset when it has dislocated from its place.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	of shoulder dislocation
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	You should know that the shoulder can dislocate in three ways:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	one is when it dislocates to the part of the axilla below;et l’aultre est qu’ele desalue en haut, selonc la guarde de la chiée, tant qu’ele soit au dessus de la
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	and the second is at the bottom of the foot;
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	and occasionally it dislocates from above, and this rarely happens;
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	and it does not dislocate behind the shoulder, and it does not dislocate within for the nerves;
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	and sometimes it dislocates underneath towards the armpit, especially in those who are thin, for in them it is very dangerous;
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	in those who are fat, it dislocates easily, and goes back in easily.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And occasionally it happens to some people that they experience a blow or fracture, and the shoulder swells from a hot abscess, and they think it is dislocated because of this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	Therefore, you must test it to be certain;et si tu le veux esprouver adonques faiz ainsi: prends un crot de fer et met il adonques sus li piez ou li main, et
et adonques encomence la cure.	and then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	And you will know it is a dislocation when it is lower towards the armpit, and there will be a difference between the sick shoulder and the healthy one, and you will find a clear difference between them;
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	you will find a hollow at the top of the shoulder, and underneath it, at the bottom of the socket, the head of the shoulder, as if it were an egg.
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	and the patient cannot bring his hand to his nose, nor move in any way;
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	and also, if it is dislocated in the upper part, it will not be hidden, for you will see it clearly at the socket;
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	and this kind of dislocation is not difficult to fix when it is new, as long as the child is not sick.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	And the method is for the minister to lift the hand of the patient up, then place your fingers underneath the socket, and raise the joint forcefully into place.
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	and the minister lifts the hand, and extends it upward, then puts it back under the socket;
si venra hastanment.	it will come quickly.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	And if it does not come as we have said within a few days after, then the patient must be bathed in warm water.
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	and the administrator should apply softening and soothing ointments, such as a decoction of alder and fenugreek and melilot in water, and it should be applied.
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	Then the patient should be laid on his back, and a pillow of wool that is neither too soft nor too hard should be placed underneath the shoulder blade, then the patient should put their heel on the pillow, and the practitioner should gently lift the shoulder and pull the hand of the affected arm.
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	And another assistant holds the head of the patient so that it does not move downward.
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	That shoulder will return immediately, and if you see that it is reset according to this manner:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	And you should have a man who is larger than the patient present.
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	and be straight towards the side, and push his shoulder under the armpit of the sick person, and lift the armpit up, so that the sick person hangs from his arm;
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	and another minister pulls the hand of the sick person downward toward the belly.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	And if the dislocation is too slight, one may use something heavy with it, and the dislocation will return immediately.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	And they reset it in another way:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	and they put a long charcoal in the ground, so that the shoulder is as hot as a pistol, neither too hot nor too cold;
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	then it is placed under the patient, but he must have a woolen cloth over him, and the patient must be still from the long heat of the fire;
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	then let his hand be extended downward on the opposite side, and the joint will return to its place gradually;
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	and if it does not want to return for all the things we have said, then do this treatment:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	take a brand two arms long and four fingers wide, which has its head pointed to go deep under the shoulder, according to this shape:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	then tie woolen cloth over the head of the brand so that the brand does not burn the patient, then put it under the shoulder of the patient;
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	and extends his arm above the long staff, and rests the shoulder on the staff, and the arm at the head of the hand, then places the arm on the sole of a large shoe, and the hand should be extended downward, and the body hanging from the other side:
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	the joint will now return.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when it is in place, however it may be, you should place under the shoulder blade a woolen sphere that is equal in size, then apply the prepared plaster of mill powder with incense and egg white over the entire shoulder and around it; then tighten it under the shoulder blade gradually, and tie the string onto the plaster, and hold the hand to their neck, and let the hand remain like this.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	And it is necessary that he eats little, until the limbs are comfortable, because he will heal faster;
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	and then eat more after 5 or 7 days, and move him;
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	and if he is stiff and not relaxed, then he is healed.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	And if the joint has been dislocated due to moisture or any other cause, you should apply fire cautery at three openings, as described in the chapter on cautery.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	And if you do all this, and it dislocates after 7 days, and the joint does not hold, and he cannot raise his arm upward, then know that the nerve at the head of the shoulder is cut or stretched or softened;
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	and know that the joint is never completely healed in its place.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	Dislocations that are towards the bottom, and in the breasts, or behind, are caused by pushing and stretching with the hands, and they are ministered to elsewhere.
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat until it is healed.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And if after healing there is stiffness in the limb, and with movement it is delayed, then let the patient use the bath many times until that stiffness is alleviated and returns to its original nature.
de la dislocation dou coute	from dislocation of the neck
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	Know that the joint of the neck is dislocated by fingers, and by fingers it is reset;
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	and if it is dislocated all over, especially in front and behind, and the dislocation is not reset, for one can see and feel it;
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	and is dislocated according to each form.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	And when you join the sick armpit with the healthy one, then you can see it clearly.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	Because the joint is stiff, and cannot bend the arm or touch its shoulder at all.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	And you should reset it as hot abscesses come, for if hot abscesses come, then it will be harmful to reset it;
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	and by chance it may not be able to be reset completely, especially when it is at the back;
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	It is worse than other dislocations, and causes greater pain, and sometimes brings about death.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And the restoration, when it can be performed, is to extend the affected limb with both your hands:
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	and the arms should be stretched out, and the hands turned according to the cut, inside and outside, and the joint pushed back into its socket, or at the root of the palm, until it returns to its place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if the dislocation is in front, it returns when he bends his hand towards his hand, and stretches from the root of the palm where it is dislocated.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	And if it does not return to its place, then apply strong extension:et li tiens la main que tu veis qu’ele soit adonsée de son leu a sa fin,
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	and let one assistant hold the hand that you see is dislocated from its place to its end, and let two assistants stretch the arm, and let them hold it steady so it does not move during the extension;et li tu tiens la main que te veis qu’ele soit adonsée a son leu, et al
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	and you hold the hand that you see is dislocated, and then turn the arm in each direction after you have wrapped a long and wide cloth around it;et si est que un le tient en la main et al’auter en la palme, et li tiens les piés ou qu
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	and when the physician examines a joint in his hand, he should apply oil to soften the joint, then bend it properly until it heals.
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	and when it is in place, he should apply a dry poultice with egg white, and hold it firmly, and bind the arm to the neck of the patient, and leave it for several days, then loosen it.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	And if the joint is firm in its place, he should loosen the binding and leave it.
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	And if you see that the joint is not setting well, then restart the poultice and binding, and leave it for several days until it is firmly set.
puis le deslie.	Then loosen it.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	And if he feels pain after the joint is reset and it moves, then bathe and massage it well, and press until the pain subsides.
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	place a fatty lamb's tail on the joint, then leave it for a day and night, then remove it, and have the patient enter the bath.
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	and when he sweats, gently rub the joint, then put the tail back on, and then enter the bath again;
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do this two or three times until he is healed.
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	if you see, place warm cow manure on it with butter and press it onto the joint;
si revenra a sa disposition.	it will return to its natural state.
li dislocation de la main	dislocation of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	Healing of the hand's joint is quick, more so than other joints.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	Nevertheless, it must be reset gently, in the same hour that it was dislocated, so that the joint does not become swollen or develop a hot abscess.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	And the reset is that you place the affected hand on a table, and someone pulls the hand, and you check to make sure it's even, and then press down on the area around the joint so that it returns to its natural state.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	Nevertheless, you must check if it is in its proper place.
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	Then have the patient lie on his back on a table and stretch out his arm.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	And if the dislocation is on the back of the hand, then have the patient lay his hand flat on a table, and with his other hand he should press down on the area around the joint.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	If it goes back into place now, that is good.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	If not, apply soothing poultices to the joint and leave it be without moving it again.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	And if he cannot bear it, and you cannot put it back into place after a few days, then the joint will remain dislocated.
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	And it does not harm the patient as long as the limb is weakened and he cannot use his hand for anything:
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	then you know that the nerves are cut or the arteries.
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	There is nothing else to do except to cauterize the area around the joint, and perhaps there is no other cure.S’il le fait, il est a l’homme; si non, il doit morier.
